[2026-07-15] - Invented-values audit, wave 4: repair, traps, stamina regen
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Tinker repair rebuilt to Source-X Use_Repair (CCharUse.cpp:792-852):
        difficulty = the item's SKILLMAKE craft-skill level scaled by damage
        percent (floor: level/4) rolled against THAT craft skill; success
        restores FULL durability; failure rolls 1/6 max-durability loss, else
        1/3 one-point chip. The old invented formulas (fixed 20-90 difficulty
        vs blanket Tinkering, skill/25 restore, 10% fail damage) are gone.

FIXED - RemoveTrap: difficulty is rand(95) (CCharSkill.cpp:2913) and a botched
        disarm deals the trap's OWN damage value, default 2 (CItem.cpp:5507) —
        not an invented 5-19 roll.

FIXED - Stamina regen is a flat max(1, REGENVAL) per tick like hits/mana
        (Source-X Stats_GetRegenVal) — the invented dex/30 (players) and
        maxStam/20 (NPCs) scaling made big creatures recover far too fast.

NOTES - Verified as genuine Source-X (citations added, no change): healing
        difficulties 85+25/50+50/0-80 (CCharSkill.cpp:2836), Focus regen
        bonuses /100 stam /200 mana (Skill_Focus), NPC book fallback = the
        classic 64-spell magery window still gated by the book's spell bits.

[2026-07-15] - Invented-values audit, wave 3: skill gain, unarmed damage, NPC skill, tools
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Skill gain followed an invented (1000-skill)/5 curve whenever a skill
        def lacked ADV_RATE. Source-X GetChancePercent: no curve = no gain.
        The substitute curve is removed; gain strictly follows ADV_RATE.

FIXED - Unarmed damage came from an invented Str/4 formula. Source-X
        Fight_CalcDamage uses the CHARDEF's DAM line (players: c_man DAM=1,4
        classic fists); a chardef with no DAM has attackBase 0. STR now only
        contributes the era damage-bonus percent.

FIXED - Skill-less NPCs no longer get an invented stat*10 combat-skill floor
        (min 25.0): Source-X fights at the raw chardef skill, so an
        under-scripted NPC hits at 0 skill instead of being silently buffed.

FIXED - Gathering tools without UsesRemaining broke at an invented 1-in-50
        per-use chance. Source-X damages the tool's HITPOINTS by 1
        (CCharSkill.cpp:2447) — a tool whose def has no hitpoints never wears.

NOTES - Verified as genuine Source-X values (citations added, no change):
        spider-web strength 60+rand(250) (CCharUse.cpp:638), NPC flee steps 20
        (CCharNPCAct.cpp:412), base wrestling swing speed 50 (CResourceCalc.cpp:49).

[2026-07-15] - Invented-values audit, wave 2: loot/summons/prices/hunger/spawn windows
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Synthetic NPC loot removed: every kill also minted stat-tier gold,
        reagents and gems ON TOP of the script-defined loot, inflating the

        define — that path (MaterializeDeathLoot) remains.

FIXED - Necromancy summons (Animate Dead, Vengeful Spirit) had flat invented
        stats (60/60/40/20, 80/80/60/40 + 60.0/80.0 skills). Summons now take
        the creature's own chardef — name, brain and the @Create stat block —
        like Source-X NPC_LoadScript, then spawn at full vitals.

FIXED - Vendor price fallback derived from the ART TILE ID (BaseId/10+5) when
        an item had no PRICE tag. Both the display and the server-side check
        now price from the itemdef VALUE (Source-X GetMakeValue).

FIXED - Item quality defaulted to 50; Source-X starts at 0 (only crafting sets
        it). Saver now persists only non-zero QUALITY.

FIXED - Invented "starvation bite" removed: a starved character lost stam/hp
        every hunger tick. Source-X starvation only halts regeneration.

FIXED - Spawner default respawn windows aligned to Source-X CCSpawn (random
        1..30 minutes when MOREP declares nothing): char spawners used a fixed
        15-30 min window, item spawners refilled in 1-5 minutes (up to 6x too

[2026-07-14] - Invented-values audit, wave 1: combat/poison/decay/caps/training
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Weapon with no DAM in its def derived damage from the ART TILE ID
        (BaseId/10 — high-graphic items hit absurdly hard). Source-X

FIXED - Two leftover synthetic-durability-50 paths: tinker REPAIR and the script
        DAMAGE verb both invented (and persisted!) a 50-point pool onto items

        into breakable ones. Both now follow Source-X: no hitpoints, no wear.

        CCharAct.cpp:4229): charges 3/3/6/6/8 (was invented 5..20), tick delay
        2/3/4/5/5s (was inverted 4s..1.5s), damage = % of max STR per level

FIXED - Ground item decay was hardcoded to 10 minutes; sphere.ini DecayTimer was

FIXED - Container caps aligned to Source-X: CONTAINERMAXITEMS default 255
        (MAX_ITEMS_CONT; was 125 config / 500 hard ceiling), BANKMAXITEMS 1000

FIXED - NPC paid training used invented 100%/30.0-cap and disagreed with the

[2026-07-14] - Field-report batch: spawn distance/LOS, boot stat repair, resource
               gem lifecycle, mounted skill animations, item durability
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Spawner children scattered up to 15 tiles from the gem:
  - Source-X loads MOREZ verbatim (0 = spawn adjacent, MoveNear dist 1); the
    component kept its 15-tile default whenever MOREZ was 0. Children now also
    require line of sight back to the spawn point (Source-X CCSpawn), so they
    cannot materialize behind walls.

FIXED - NPCs with STR=0 persisted by older builds:
  - Saves written before the OSTR fix baked STR=0 into native format, beyond
    the loader fix and RESPAWN FULL (non-spawner NPCs). Boot repair now restores
    base stats from the O-mirror or re-runs the chardef @Create, then tops off
    vitals ([boot_repair] log line).

FIXED - Resource-marker worldgems lived forever (TIMER=-1):
  - Fishing/mining/lumberjack markers only armed a decay once fully depleted and
    cleared it while regenerating — one immortal invisible item per worked tile.
    Now every touch re-arms decay one regen period out (Source-X MoveToDecay
    lifecycle: by expiry the vein is fully refilled, so deletion is lossless).
    Boot repair arms decay on markers already saved without one.

FIXED - Skill animations dismounted/remounted the rider visually:
  - Fishing/mining/lumberjack swings sent the on-foot animation for mounted
    characters. Skill animations now use the mounted variant (shared
    BodyAnimTranslator.ToMounted, same table the spell-cast path used).

FIXED - Weapons/armor without HITPOINTS broke and vanished:
  - The combat wear path synthesized a default durability for items whose def
    defines none — classic packs define HITPOINTS on almost nothing, so all
    gear slowly self-destructed. Source-X only wears items that actually have
    hitpoints; the synthetic assignment is removed.

ADDED - Item destruction emote:
  - When worn gear breaks, everyone nearby sees "*<item> is destroyed*" over
    the wearer (Source-X ITEM_DMG_DESTROYED emote) in addition to the owner's
    private message.

[2026-07-14] - RESPAWN FULL admin command
----------------------------------------

ADDED - RESPAWN FULL (console/telnet/.serv.respawn full): kills every spawner's
        children first, then refills fresh. Plain RESPAWN only tops missing
        children up, so NPCs materialized in a broken state by an older build
        stayed in the world; FULL replaces them all in one pass.

[2026-07-14] - Legacy stat load (OSTR->STR) and spawn vitals top-off
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Every NPC loaded from a classic Sphere save had base stats of 0:
  - Classic saves persist only OSTR/ODEX/OINT; Source-X r_LoadVal maps those to
    Stat_SetBase — the same slot as STR/DEX/INT. WorldLoader mirrored them into
    the O-fields only, so Str/Dex/Int stayed 0 after load. This zeroed combat
    math worldwide: the relative-strength morale term made stat-0 monsters
    afraid of everything (they ignored valid targets such as a dismounted
    mount and only fought via retaliation memories). OSTR/ODEX/OINT now seed
    the base stats exactly like STR/DEX/INT.

FIXED - Spawner-created NPCs materialized at 1 hp:
  - Classic packs assign STR/DEX/INT inside the chardef's @Create block, which
    raises the max vitals AFTER SpawnComponent seeded them from the stat-less
    section header — a fresh orc arrived at 1/102 hp. The spawn pipeline now
    tops off Hits/Stam/Mana after @Create, same as the .add pipeline.

ADDED - Regression tests: classic O-stat load, live-pack orc spawn (name from
        #NAMES_, @Create stat ranges, full vitals), dismounted mount remains a
        valid monster target.

[2026-07-14] - Script trigger leaked across sections (fishing pole dclick dead)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - A trigger fired by name could execute an ON= block belonging to a LATER,
        unrelated definition in the same .scp file:
  - TriggerRunner's on-demand file scan opened the resource at its stored section
    header but then searched EVERY section to end-of-file for the trigger. Any
    definition without its own handler silently inherited the next same-named
    ON= block below it. Live symptom: double-clicking i_fishing_pole did nothing —
    [ITEMDEF 0dbf] has no @DClick, so the scan drifted into the arrow-shaft def's
    "@DClick ... RETURN 1" further down sphere_item_profession.scp, blocking both
    the dclick-equip and the fishing target. Trigger search is now confined to
    the resource's own section (Source-X CResourceLock stops at the next
    [header]). Live-pack regression probes added (FishingPoleLivePackProbe).

[2026-07-14] - net_in stall attribution and follower-count scan cache
----------------------------------------

ADDED - [slow_packet] diagnostic: a single inbound packet handler running longer
        than SlowPacketWarnMs (new sphere.ini key, default 20, 0=off) logs the
        opcode, handler name and duration. [loop_stall] lines now also carry
        pkts= (packets handled that pass) and slowest_pkt=0x??@ms, so a stall in
        the net_in phase names its dominant packet instead of an opaque total.

CHANGED - CurFollower no longer walks the whole world on every read:
  - The follower count recomputed by scanning ALL world objects (100K+ on large
    saves, plus a full array copy per call), and the status packet (0x11, sent
    on every 0x34 status request) reads it. The scan result is now cached for
    2 seconds; pet ownership changes (SetOwnerControllerRaw) and mount/dismount
    (Ridden flag transitions) invalidate the owner's cache so follower-cap
    checks never act on a stale count. Source-X maintains a stored counter
    (CCharUse.cpp GetCurFollowers) and never scans, so caching is strictly
    closer to reference behavior.

[2026-07-14] - Map-edge spawn crash fix (multicore fallback trigger)
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - [slow_tick] / [loop_stall] diagnostic warnings are now configurable and
          less chatty:
  - The fixed 25ms / 50ms thresholds warned on routine GC and network-flush blips
    (a 30ms tick is under a third of the 100ms tick budget). New sphere.ini keys
    SlowTickWarnMs (default 50) and LoopStallWarnMs (default 100) set the
    thresholds; 0 disables that warning entirely.

FIXED - IndexOutOfRangeException in SpawnComponent.FindSpawnPosition crashed the
        multicore tick and forced a 30s single-thread fallback:
  - A spawner within spawn-range of the map edge can roll a candidate position
    with a negative X/Y. In MapReader/UopMapReader.GetCell, -3 / 8 truncates to
    block 0 (passing the block bounds check) while -3 % 8 = -3 indexed the cell
    array with a negative offset, throwing. Both readers now reject off-map
    coordinates and return a default cell, and FindSpawnPosition rejects off-map
    candidates up front (Source-X IsValidPoint gate) and retries instead.

[2026-07-14] - Standing-Z desync fix and map-static door auto-close
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Character elevation desynced from the client, causing a spurious fall sound
        and a Z snap on double-click:
  - The per-step walk path seats a character on the averaged land-tile center (the
    same value the client and Source-X derive), but the seat/correction path
    (login, dismount, mount, teleport) used a second algorithm that returned the raw
    NW-corner tile Z instead. On sloped land these disagree, so the stored Z drifted
    off the surface the client renders. The drift stayed hidden until a self-update
    (0x20) re-imposed it — which a double-click sends when the character turns to
    face the used object — snapping the character up (near building floors) or down
    (on open slopes). The same drift made the next walk step re-derive the true
    center, tripping the client's fall "Ouch" with no real height change. The seat
    path now derives land Z from the averaged tile center, matching the walk path.

ADDED - Map-static doors now auto-close after 20 seconds, matching item doors:
  - Doors baked into the map statics (as opposed to real item-doors) were tracked
    only as an open-overlay set and never received the item timer that swings a door
    shut, so they stayed open indefinitely. They now carry the same 20s auto-close
    deadline (Source-X Use_Door timer); a post-tick pass swings the expired ones
    shut and broadcasts the close to nearby clients.


[2026-07-13] - Consumable single-use, pile-merge cap, and scissors data-loss fixes
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Consuming a stacked item destroyed the whole pile and could delete a fixture:
  - Booze and potions deleted the entire stack on a single use, and none of the
    eat/drink handlers checked movability first, so one sip wiped a pile and
    double-clicking a placed keg/pitcher/food decoration (a Move_Never fixture)
    destroyed it. They now consume exactly one unit (Source-X Use_Eat/Use_Drink,
    wConsume=1) and refuse an item the user cannot move instead of destroying it.

FIXED - Merging one stack onto another mis-handled the size cap and remainder:
  - The merge grew a pile up to the raw 65535 amount ceiling instead of the target's
    effective stack limit (per-item MAXAMOUNT override or ITEMSMAXAMOUNT, Source-X
    GetMaxAmount), so a pile could exceed its configured cap. It now caps at the
    target's MaxAmount and the overflow remainder is preserved beside the pile.
  - Dropping a stack onto a matching pile is a merge, not an insert into a container,
    so it is no longer gated by the destination's container item-count / weight /
    nesting caps. Previously the container weight cap wrongly rejected large stacks
    (e.g. dropping 5000 gold onto a ground pile when the container weight limit is
    lower). A remainder whose target's parent lookup fails now bounces to the target's
    top-level tile instead of being duplicated.

FIXED - Scissors could delete a bloody-bandage stack and cut a fixture:
  - Cutting a stack of bloody bandages deleted it; it now cleans the stack back to
    plain bandages (type convert, whole stack kept). Scissors also refuse a
    Move_Never cloth fixture instead of type-converting it.


[2026-07-13] - World consistency auditor and boot-time canary
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Post-load world invariant auditor with a boot-time consistency canary:
  - A single read-only pass over the loaded world flags the class of "looks fine in
    the property editor but broken on the client" inconsistencies that only surface
    with the real pack and save: a container whose client-facing index disagrees
    with its authoritative contents (an empty-looking bag), an item whose raw type
    was never materialised from its definition, a contained item with no parent, and
    a char spawner tracking far more live children than its cap. The server now runs
    it right after world load and logs a summary (clean, or the anomaly counts and
    first offenders), so these surface in the log instead of only in-game. The same
    checks back a test that audits the live pack+save when present and skips in CI.
  - Diagnostics-only sweeps added alongside: a double-click pass over every item
    type (asserting nothing crashes or is wrongly destroyed) and a headless-bot
    check that flags an item vanishing from view while the bot stands still (the
    client-side symptom of an object being desynced out of view).


[2026-07-13] - Item @Create on materialization, spawner child re-link, invisible-item double-click
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Loot/spawn items never ran their itemdef @Create trigger, so magic items came out inert:
  - A magic weapon's magic (damage bonus, magic attribute, hit points, magic hue)
    lives entirely in its itemdef @Create block. Source-X fires @Create on every
    item it materialises from a def (loot, spawn, NEWITEM, vendor restock, carve,
    .add); SphereNet never did, so a rolled magic def produced a named-but-inert
    item. ApplyInstanceMetadata now fires the @Create trigger once per fresh
    instance through a wired hook, guarded so re-stamping metadata cannot compound
    the effect, and the world load never routes through it (reloaded items keep
    their persisted state and do not re-fire).

FIXED - Char spawners forgot their live children on reload and respawned their whole quota:
  - The re-link that restores a spawner's current spawned-children count from its
    saved ADDOBJ entries only ran for classic SPAWNID-tagged spawners. A native
    MORE1/AMOUNT spawner has no SPAWNID, so on reload its child count reset to zero,
    it saw current-count below its cap, and it respawned a fresh quota every restart
    — the population near one spawn point grew without bound. The re-link now runs
    inside spawn-component init for every char spawner (matching the reference
    rebuilding current-spawned purely from ADDOBJ). It never alters the cap, which
    stays the AMOUNT field; any excess carried from an over-accumulated save drains
    off by attrition.

FIXED - A GM double-clicking an invisible spawner made it vanish from view instead of triggering:
  - Invisible items (spawn worldgems, triggers) are sent to a client with AllShow
    OR GM privilege, but the double-click and skill-target can-see gates only
    honoured AllShow. A GM who legitimately saw an invisible spawner double-clicked
    it, the server judged it unseeable, and "corrected" the client by removing it
    from view — the item looked deleted (it was untouched server-side) and the
    spawner never fired. Both gates now use the same audience as the view send
    (AllShow OR GM), so the double-click reaches the spawner and produces a spawn.


[2026-07-13] - Movement pacing, container index on load, item type materialization, double-click gaps
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Saved container contents were invisible to the client after a restart:
  - The container reverse index (read by the client's open-container batch) is
    maintained by the Item.ContainedIn setter, which only updates the index once the
    world resolver is wired — but the initial save load ran BEFORE that wiring. Every
    contained item therefore landed in its parent's Contents (visible to the property
    editor) yet never entered the index, so bags rendered empty on the client while
    still holding their items server-side. The world resolver is now wired before the
    load, and WorldLoader rebuilds the index once from the authoritative ContainedIn
    at the end of the load.

FIXED - A legacy item's TYPE and TDATA were not applied to the instance:
  - A save stores neither TYPE nor TDATA — an item's type is defined by its ITEMDEF.
    The lazy type getter resolved it, but the raw type field stayed at its default, so
    the <TYPE> script read, the property editor, and every code path that reads the raw
    type directly (spellbook/book/map/ship/multi/container checks, static blocking,
    content-by-type search) saw t_normal. TYPE/TDATA are now materialized from the
    resolved definition after load, matching a script-created item, and the TYPE
    property resolves through the definition. The save format is unchanged.

CHANGED - Movement pacing aligned to Source-X (fixes an on-foot in-combat stutter):
  - Removed the 20% war-mode foot-movement penalty. Neither the 2D client nor Source-X
    applies a combat-stance walk penalty; pacing the server slower than the client
    sends saturated the client's unconfirmed-step budget and produced a repeating
    stutter while running on foot in war mode.
  - The next allowed walk is now paced 30ms early (Source-X Event_CheckWalkBuffer iDelay
    offset) so player ping/jitter does not false-throttle a legitimately timed step. The
    walk-token bucket still caps the sustained rate.

ADDED - Double-click behavior for grain, grass and water troughs:
  - t_grain and t_grass are eaten and t_water_wash (water troughs/basins) are drunk
    from, restoring hunger, matching Source-X Use_Eat/Use_Drink. Previously these fell
    through to the generic "can't think of a way to use that" default. A placed fixture
    is never consumed; only a movable stack loses a unit.


[2026-07-13] - House/ship region events on load; server tick aligned to Source-X
----------------------------------------

FIXED - House and ship region scripts (@Enter/@Step/...) were not applied after load:
  - A dynamically realized house or ship region carried its EVENTS only as a
    REGION.EVENTS tag on the multi item; the tag round-tripped through save but was
    never turned into region events, so the region's @Enter/@Step triggers never
    fired. House and ship region creation now parses REGION.EVENTS into the region's
    event list (comma-separated, leading '+' trimmed, de-duplicated) using the same
    key form TriggerDispatcher resolves, so the scripts fire on entry/step again.

CHANGED - World-loop tick interval now matches Source-X exactly:
  - The tick (ServerTickMs) default is 100ms (10 ticks/s), matching Source-X
    MSECS_PER_TICK (TICKS_PER_SEC=10) instead of the previous 20 ticks/s. Regen and
    timer cadence now advance on the reference unit. Network I/O and the movement
    queue still drain every main-loop iteration, so responsiveness is unchanged; only
    world-simulation timing is aligned. Configurable via the ServerTickMs ini key
    (clamped to [20,250]).


[2026-07-13] - Spell-effect memory items; synthetic-index resolution sweep
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Active spell effects are mirrored as worn IT_SPELL memory items:
  - When a durational effect is applied, an item carrying the spell (graphic from the
    spell's RUNE_ITEM, spell id in MOREX, strength in MOREY, caster in LINK) is equipped
    on the hidden memory layer, matching Source-X CChar::Spell_Effect_Create. It is
    visible to GM .edit and deleted on every effect removal; the active-effect list
    stays authoritative for stat deltas and expiry. Hidden from the client (buff icon is
    the visible feedback). Persistence is unchanged: the item is not double-saved, and it
    is recreated from the effect record on load; the save-time stat unwind no longer
    deletes it.

FIXED - Named definitions resolving to Type/graphic 0 (synthetic-index truncation):
  - A non-numeric definition header ([ITEMDEF i_xxx], [CHARDEF c_xxx]) is keyed by a
    synthetic 24-bit index above 0xFFFF. Several paths truncated it to 16 bits and then
    looked the definition up by the truncated value, missing it and reading Type/TData/
    MORE as 0. Fixed across:
    - Legacy item load: a [WORLDITEM i_xxx] with a non-numeric ITEMDEF header now pins
      the defname as an ITEMDEF tag, so the instance recovers its Type/TData from the
      real definition instead of the 16-bit graphic. MORE1 display uses the resolved
      type so a spawn item shows its defname.
    - Item spawners: ItemSpawnComponent kept the target item-def index in a ushort;
      widened to the full 32-bit index so a spawner targeting a named itemdef resolves
      the correct def and no longer rejects synthetic indices.
    - SERV.NEWITEM: now applies the full item-def metadata (graphic, type, tags) instead
      of a raw 16-bit cast.
    - Spell RUNE_ITEM/SCROLL_ITEM/EFFECT_ID: a defname now resolves through the item
      def's display graphic (DisplayIdRef chain) instead of the truncated resource
      index, fixing corrupt rune/scroll/effect graphics for the necromancy/AOS spells.
  - Audited region/area/room types, EVENTS/TEVENTS, dialogs, functions, typedefs, menus
    and speech: all resolve by full-width key and were already correct.

[2026-07-13] - Container display, worn-item load, spawn body, deed placement
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Contained items missing from the client container view (present in .edit):
  - Opening a container (SendOpenContainer) and refreshing the backpack now send the
    whole content list as a single 0x3C batch (Source-X CClient::addContainerContents
    / PacketItemContents), instead of one 0x25 per child. ClassicUO's 0x25 handler
    silently drops any item whose container entity it does not yet know; a per-item
    stream could lose children while they still existed server-side. The batch is
    processed atomically (client clears and rewrites the list), matching the reference.
    The server-side _contents list and the container reverse index were already fully
    consistent on load (verified against a 92k-item save); the defect was in the wire
    format, not the data.

FIXED - Worn clothing/weapons dropping under NPCs or leaving NPCs naked:
  - Classic Sphere saves store worn gear as CONT=<char> with no LAYER when the itemdef
    also lacks one (TYPE=t_clothing); the layer now derives from tiledata (the graphic
    Quality byte, matching Source-X CItemBase m_layer), then from the item type
    (hair/beard/container) as a final fallback.
  - EquipLoadedItem no longer evicts an already-worn item: a tiledata-derived layer
    that collides with an occupied slot sends the newcomer to the backpack instead of
    bouncing the incumbent to the ground (the "weapon in hand and a weapon dropped
    underneath" case).
  - ITEMDEF DUPEITEM now inherits Type/Layer/TDATA from the master itemdef, so items
    defined only as a dupe (e.g. a fishing pole variant) resolve their real type and
    equip layer instead of Type=0.

FIXED - Spawned NPCs named Spawn_FFFF with body 0xFFFF:
  - Non-numeric CHARDEF headers (e.g. [CHARDEF c_alchemist]) receive a synthetic 24-bit
    definition index above 0xFFFF. The spawn component clamped it to 0xFFFF, producing a
    nameless body-0xFFFF creature; it now carries the full index and resolves the body
    through CharDefHelper.ResolveBodyId (DispIndex alias chain).

FIXED - Character Z jumped on the first double-click without moving:
  - Login/entry Z snapping to the surface no longer applies a fixed tolerance cap; the
    server places the character on the effective surface Z on entry, matching the height
    the client would otherwise correct to (Source-X addPlayerView behavior).

FIXED - Ship deed placement rejected valid multis ("cannot place house here"):
  - Deed-to-multi resolution now accepts multi id 0 (a valid multi.mul index) and
    resolves the multi from the deed's MORE/MORE1 defname tag via the multi registry,
    with the ship class detected from the deed graphic.

[2026-07-13] - Legacy save load order and staff item visibility
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Legacy NPCs loaded invisible from classic Sphere saves:
  - Char/item/spell definitions are now built (DefinitionLoader.LoadAll) before the
    world save is loaded, instead of after. Legacy Sphere saves store an NPC's body
    only in the [WORLDCHAR <defname>] section header, resolved through the definition
    tables; loading definitions afterwards left every such NPC at body 0 (invisible,
    though its name still resolved from the save) and left spawn items without their
    ITEMDEF type inheritance. Item graphics survived only because item id resolution
    has a defname-index fallback that character body resolution lacks.

CHANGED - Staff visibility of invisible items:
  - GM and higher now see ATTR_INVIS items (spawn worldgems, triggers, and similar)
    rendered dimmed even with AllShow off, so staff can audit spawners on sight.
    Normal players remain gated by AllShow.

ADDED - CLAUDE.md contributor/agent guide at the repository root.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirty-sixth batch (suit max-pool aggregation)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Effective max hit/mana/stamina from equipped items (Wave 264):
  - A character's effective maximum hit/mana/stamina pool is now the stored base
    pool plus the sum of the matching item bonus across every equipped item,
    using the Source-X property names BONUSHITSMAX/BONUSMANAMAX/BONUSSTAMMAX
    (BONUSHITS in Source-X is a separate regeneration field, not a max bonus).
  - The max-pool getters report the effective total, so the status/paperdoll and
    health bars, the ceilings that healing and regeneration fill toward, and the
    ratio checks all stay consistent. The current pool can be healed up into the
    suit bonus while the piece is worn.
  - Unequipping a max-pool piece clamps the current pool down to the reduced
    maximum, matching the reference stat-mod behavior.
  - The stored base pool is what the world save serializes; the suit contribution
    is derived on read and never written back as base, so it cannot compound
    across save cycles. Old saves with a zeroed max still trigger the login
    backfill unchanged.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirty-fifth batch (suit stat aggregation)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Effective STR/DEX/INT from equipped items (Wave 263):
  - A character's effective strength/dexterity/intelligence is now the base stat
    plus the sum of the matching item bonus (BONUSSTR/BONUSDEX/BONUSINT) across
    every equipped item, derived on read (no equip-time mutation, floored at 0),
    the same live-scan approach as the resist slice.
  - The consumers that reflect the suit now read the effective stat: the
    status/paperdoll STR/DEX/INT, melee strength damage (unarmed base and the
    per-era strength damage bonus), carry weight (max weight now scales with the
    strength suit, with the movement overload check and the status max-weight
    unified onto a single source), the equip strength-requirement gate, and the
    stat contribution to adjusted skill.
  - The stored max hit/mana/stamina pools stay derived from the base stat, so a
    stat suit never inflates them; the base stat field and the STR/DEX/INT script
    property keep reporting the base. Max-pool item bonuses (BONUSHITS and the
    like) are intentionally left for a separate pass.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirty-fourth batch (suit resist aggregation)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Effective elemental resist from equipped items (Wave 262):
  - A character's effective fire/cold/poison/energy/physical resist is now the
    base resist plus the sum of the same resist across every equipped item,
    derived on read (no equip-time mutation, so the base stays pristine and
    nothing is written to the save). Combat damage resolution, poison ticks and
    the status/paperdoll display all use the effective suit total; the stored
    base field and the RESxxx script property keep reporting the base.
  - Stat (STR/DEX/INT) and max-hits/mana/stam item bonuses are intentionally not
    aggregated yet (they feed derived values and need a separate pass).

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirty-third batch (Necromancy school)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Necromancy spell school (Waves 254-261):
  - The Necromancy school is now functionally complete (16 of 17 spells; only
    Exorcism is left, which the Source-X reference itself leaves unimplemented).
  - Debuffs: Corpse Skin shifts elemental resists; Mind Rot raises the victim's
    spell mana cost by 10%.
  - A generic periodic damage-over-time engine drives Pain Spike (fixed direct
    damage over ten ticks) and Strangle (poison that accelerates and scales with
    the victim's fatigue). In-flight ticks are not persisted across a restart.
  - Damage reactions on the victim side: Blood Oath reflects a bonded enemy's
    blow back at it (and hurts the victim slightly more); Evil Omen makes the
    next harmful hit land harder (+25% melee, or one poison level), then is spent.
  - Area damage: Poison Strike hits the primary in full and splashes half within
    two tiles; Wither deals cold damage to everything within four tiles of the
    caster.
  - Forms: Lich Form and Vampiric Embrace shift resists; Vampiric Embrace also
    leeches life on any hit. One polymorph-layer form is active at a time.
  - Summons: Vengeful Spirit raises a revenant that hunts the target; Animate
    Dead raises an undead from a targeted corpse (a humanoid corpse yields a
    zombie, a creature corpse its own kind); Summon Familiar summons a default
    familiar. Summons are caster-owned, conjured and time-limited.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirty-second batch (deferred groups)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Owned-vendor cash dispense and restock faucet fix (Wave 251):
  - The "cash" pet command now empties an owned vendor's purse into the owner's
    pack (Source-X NPC_VendorGetChkVerb PC_CASH). To prevent a free-gold faucet,
    the periodic restock no longer tops up an owned vendor's purse - only plain
    shopkeepers keep the infinite buy fund; owned vendors accumulate real earnings
    only. The bought/samples/stock verbs no longer raise a bogus target cursor.

ADDED - Effective-skill layer (Wave 252):
  - GetAdjustedSkill now includes the per-character SkillMod<n> equipment bonus on
    top of the base skill and stat contribution (Source-X Skill_GetAdjusted). The
    skill window (0x3A) reports the adjusted value with the raw base as the second
    field. A SkillMod<n> script property reads/writes the bonus (bare key or TAG.
    prefix), persisted as a tag. The raw base used by combat, crafting and skill
    gain is unchanged, so existing content sees no behavior change until the bonus
    is set.

ADDED - Necromancy foundation: Curse Weapon and Wraith Form (Wave 253):
  - On a damaging melee hit, a Curse Weapon state adds its level to the weapon's
    life-leech percent (weapon-gated), and a Wraith Form state drains the target's
    mana to the attacker scaled by Spirit Speak (Source-X CCharFight on-hit hooks).
  - The Curse Weapon and Wraith Form spells set these timed states with the normal
    effect expiry, persistence and revert; the Curse Weapon level survives a
    save/load round-trip.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirty-first batch
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Account aging admin command (Wave 250):
  - ACCOUNT UNUSED <days> [DELETE] lists (or, with DELETE, removes) accounts idle
    for at least N days, based on last login or creation date (Source-X
    Cmd_ListUnused). Staff accounts are never aged out, and an online account has
    a recent last-login so it never matches. Command-driven, not automatic.

ADDED - Per-item and global stack-size cap (Wave 250):
  - MAXAMOUNT is now readable/settable on items and enforced when merging piles:
    stackable items cap at the global ItemsMaxAmount (default 60000, Source-X
    m_iItemsMaxAmount) or a per-item override; non-stackable items report 0. The
    override is saved. Previously stacks were only bounded by 65535.

ADDED - Communication crystal tooltips (Wave 250):
  - A comm crystal now shows its state on the AOS tooltip: activated (linked to
    another crystal) or deactivated, plus the broadcast line.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, thirtieth batch
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Character and item script properties (Wave 249):
  - STAMINA (alias of STAM), STATPERCENT.<stat> (a pool as a percentage of its
    adjusted max; STR maps to hits, DEX to stamina, INT to mana), BLOODCOLOR
    (blood-splatter hue), and FOLLOWERSLOTS (how many follower slots a creature
    occupies, with a script override) are now resolvable on characters.
  - BASEWEIGHT exposes and overrides an item's per-unit weight; setting it drives
    the item's total weight and carry checks. BLOODCOLOR, FOLLOWERSLOTS and
    BASEWEIGHT overrides are saved.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-ninth batch
----------------------------------------

ADDED - EquipLastWeapon client macro (Wave 248):
  - The 0xD7 0x1E "re-wield last weapon" macro is now handled. The character
    tracks the last weapon it equipped (Source-X m_uidWeaponLast); the macro
    pulls that weapon out of the player's own pack and equips it, reusing the
    normal equip path (a dropped or traded weapon can't be summoned back).

ADDED - Targeted-skill fast path (Wave 248):
  - The 0xBF 0x2E packet uses a skill against an already-picked target without a
    target-cursor round-trip. It runs the same busy/can-use checks and
    PreStart/Start trigger chain as a normal skill use, then resolves directly
    against the supplied target.

ADDED - Per-character regen amount overrides (Wave 248):
  - Characters now honour per-char REGENVALHITS/REGENVALMANA/REGENVALSTAM/
    REGENVALFOOD (Source-X Stats_GetRegenVal): the number of points recovered
    per regeneration event, effective value max(1, stored). The human +2 hit
    racial still applies on top. Saved and restored across a restart. This
    completes the per-char regen surface begun in the previous batch.

FIXED - Modern-client spell casting from the 0xBF 0x1C packet (Wave 248):
  - The client's spell-select packet (0xBF 0x1C, used by clients 6.0.1.42+) was
    mis-wired to a viewport-size handler, so spells cast from the modern client
    UI were silently dropped. Screen size already travels on 0xBF 0x05 / 0xC8, so
    the duplicate handler was dead; 0x1C now casts the selected spell.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-eighth batch
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Per-character stat regeneration rate overrides (Wave 247):
  - Characters now honour per-char REGENHITS/REGENMANA/REGENSTAM/REGENFOOD (and
    the tenths-of-a-second REGEN*D variants) rate properties, resolved the way
    Source-X CChar::Stats_GetRegenRate does: 0 falls back to the global rate, a
    positive value is the per-char delay in seconds, and a negative value disables
    regeneration of that stat. The override is saved and restored across a restart.
  - Global food decay is now driven by a configurable rate (REGEN3) instead of a
    hardcoded 60 minutes.

FIXED - Old-style menu (0x7C) TESTIF entry gating (Wave 247):
  - A skill-menu entry's TESTIF= expression was never evaluated, so entries that
    should have been hidden were always shown. The expression is now evaluated
    against the character and a false result hides the entry.

FIXED - Old-style menu could desync the client on oversized lists (Wave 247):
  - The item-count byte was clamped to 255 but the full item list was still
    written, corrupting the client's read cursor when a menu exceeded 255 entries.
    Menus are now truncated to the Source-X MAX_MENU_ITEMS limit and never write
    more items than the count byte advertises.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-seventh batch
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - Stat regeneration now matches Source-X rates (Wave 246):
  - The REGEN0/1/2 rates are now read as SECONDS to recover one point (Source-X
    m_iRegenRate * MSECS_PER_SEC), not tenths of a second, so regeneration is
    roughly 5-10x slower than before (default hit regen 40s, mana 20s, stam 10s).
  - Fixed the stat order: REGEN1 is INT/mana and REGEN2 is DEX/stam (they were
    swapped). A Source-X / mortechUO sphere.ini setting Regen1/Regen2 is now
    applied to the correct pool.
  - Hunger decay slowed from 10 minutes to 60 minutes per point (Source-X food
    rate), and the human race now regenerates +2 extra hit points per event.
  - OPERATOR NOTE: this is a deliberate, player-visible balance change toward
    Source-X parity. A shard that relied on the old fast regeneration should set
    Regen0/1/2 explicitly (in seconds) to tune it.

FIXED - GM page queue survives a restart (Wave 245):
  - Pending GM/help pages were held only in memory and were lost on every
    restart, and GMPAGE sections in an imported classic save were silently
    dropped. The queue now lives on the world (like Source-X g_World.m_GMPages)
    and is written to and read from the server-data save.

FIXED - Guild member titles containing a comma no longer drop members (Wave 245):
  - Guild members are packed into one comma-separated tag with colon-separated
    fields. Colons in a title were escaped but commas were not, so a player-set
    title containing a comma split the record on load and dropped the trailing
    members. Commas in titles are now escaped as well.

ADDED - Communication crystal player linking (Wave 245):
  - Double-clicking a communication crystal now opens a target cursor; targeting
    another communication crystal links them so speech near one is relayed to the
    other (previously only a GM script verb could link them). The relay also now
    verifies the linked partner is itself a crystal.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-fifth batch
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Guild and quest buttons use the correct 0xD7 transport (Wave 244):
  - The guild and quest button presses are sent by the client on the 0xD7
    (EXTAOS) subcommand space, not 0xBF (Source-X PacketGuildButton /
    PacketQuestButton). They were handled on 0xBF, so a real client never fired
    the @UserGuildButton / @UserQuestButton triggers. They are now handled on
    0xD7 0x28 / 0x32, and the stale 0xBF 0x28 mapping is removed.

ADDED - Gargoyle flight toggle (Wave 244):
  - 0xBF 0x32 (previously mis-mapped to the quest button) now toggles gargoyle
    flight for a living gargoyle carrying the flight racial: it flips the
    hovering state and the gargoyle-flight buff, and the flight state now rides
    the mobile-flags 0x04 bit to the player and every nearby observer (the
    hovering bit was previously never sent).

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-fourth batch
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Ship fast-mode speed scaling (Wave 243):
  - Continuous ("normal") sailing now advances twice as fast as one-tile
    steering, matching Source-X CCMultiMovable::SetNextMove which halves the
    tick interval in the fast speed mode. The ship speed mode was previously
    dead state (never set from steering input, never read in the timing path),
    so normal sailing ran at the slow rate. Tiles-per-tick was already correct.

FIXED - Pet with a loaded pack can no longer be stabled (Wave 243):
  - A pet carrying items in its backpack is refused at the stablemaster
    (matching Source-X), preventing the carried items from being lost with the
    stored snapshot. The owner must empty the pet's pack first.

ADDED - Pre-AOS wrestling special moves (Wave 243):
  - 0xBF 0x09 (disarm) and 0x0A (paralyzing blow) now fire the @UserSpecialMove
    trigger with the ability id, the same sink as the AOS special-move packet
    (0xD7 0x19).

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-third batch
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Invulnerable characters no longer take damage (Wave 242):
  - STATF_INVUL was checked at death but not at damage application, so an
    invulnerable character still lost hit points from every source. Source-X
    CChar::OnTakeDamage bounces the blow (deals zero) while invulnerable, unless
    the strike is flagged DAMAGE_GOD. A shared CombatEngine.IsDamageImmune guard
    now protects every damage site: script DAMAGE, melee (including reflected
    damage), spells, container and step traps, and field damage.

FIXED - Corpse resurrection requires a top-level corpse (Wave 242):
  - The Healing/Veterinary corpse-target resurrection now refuses a corpse that
    sits inside a container, matching Source-X CItemCorpse::IsCorpseResurrectable
    (a corpse must be a ground object). The self-resurrection path already
    enforced this.

FIXED - Region vendor restock interval unit (Wave 242):
  - The region RestockVendors tag was parsed as minutes; Source-X
    NPC_Vendor_Restock measures it in tenths of a second for legacy script
    compatibility. A legacy RestockVendors=6000 now correctly means 600 seconds
    (10 minutes) instead of 6000 minutes.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-second batch
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Line-of-sight multi and custom-house wall occlusion (Wave 241):
  - Placed house and ship walls no longer let sight (and ranged attacks) pass
    through them. The static LOS path reads MUL map statics, not the virtual
    walls of runtime-placed multis, so those were invisible to the ray. LOS now
    synthesizes multi geometry the same way the walk check does (Source-X
    LOS_NB_MULTI): both multi.mul components and committed custom-house design
    tiles occlude the ray.

ADDED - Remaining line-of-sight passes (Wave 241):
  - BLOCKLOS_HEIGHT: items whose definition carries CAN_I_BLOCKLOS_HEIGHT block
    sight even without a wall flag, on the static, dynamic and multi paths
    (shared TerrainEngine.GraphicBlocksLos helper).
  - LOS_FISHING: CanSeeLOS now takes a LosFlags argument; with LosFlags.Fishing
    the ray must stay over water once it is two or more tiles from the caster.
    Engine-level for now (the fishing skill wiring is a separate opt-in).

NOTES:
  - The deep region-crossing flags (LOS_NO_OTHER_REGION, LOS_NC_MULTI, the
    region-local LOS_NB_LOCAL_* forms) remain deferred; they need a per-cell
    region model and have minimal gameplay impact.


[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twenty-first batch
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Line-of-sight dynamic item occlusion (Wave 240):
  - The LOS ray only checked terrain and MUL statics, so an item placed in the
    world at runtime never blocked sight — a wall or crate dropped between two
    characters could be seen and shot straight through. The ray now consults
    live items along its path (Source-X CanSeeLOS_New LOS_NB_DYNAMIC): a
    wall/impassable/no-shoot item whose Z span covers the ray blocks it, exactly
    like a static.
  - Windows no longer block line of sight (Source-X LOS_NB_WINDOWS default for
    archery/magery), on both the static and dynamic paths.

NOTES:
  - Partial LOS parity: the niche flag variants (LOS_FISHING, multi-region
    occlusion / LOS_NC_MULTI, LOS_NO_OTHER_REGION, BLOCKLOS_HEIGHT, the
    region-local LOS_NB_LOCAL_* forms) remain deferred.


[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, twentieth batch
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Sector sleep model (Wave 239):
  - Sectors now decide whether they may sleep with the full Source-X
    CSector::_CanSleep model instead of a bare client-count check: sleeping is
    vetoed by SECF_NoSleep or a zero sleep-delay, blocked while a client is
    inside, granted immediately under SECF_InstaSleep, and otherwise granted
    once the sector has been clientless past the sleep-delay (default 10
    minutes). An 8-neighbour adjacency sweep keeps the ring around an active
    sector awake so a player never walks into a cold sector.
  - New SectorFlag enum (SECF_NoSleep / SECF_InstaSleep) with FLAGS / NOSLEEP /
    INSTASLEEP script access; <CANSLEEP> now reports the full model.
  - A SECF_NoSleep sector stays in the world tick set regardless of player
    proximity, and the player's sector stamps its last-client time each tick.

NOTES:
  - The engine's actual awake/asleep decision remains the spatial active-set
    (a window of sectors around each online player) rather than the temporal
    timeout; the CanSleep predicate and SECF_NoSleep behaviour are faithful,
    while InstaSleep is modelled at the predicate/script level.


[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, nineteenth batch
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Custom-house design valid-item enforcement (Wave 238):
  - The design editor accepted any non-zero tile graphic, so a crafted 0xD7
    stream could place arbitrary graphics (multi bodies, blocking statics,
    unrenderable ids) into a house. Build/Stairs/Roof now gate placement on
    Source-X CItemMultiCustom::IsValidItem: the graphic must be a real static
    item (0 < id < 0x4000), a check applied to everyone including GMs; GMs then
    bypass the piece whitelist while ordinary designers must match it.
  - HouseDesignValidItems holds an optional whitelist (Source-X
    ValidItemsContainer). Empty means range-only enforcement so custom housing
    works without the client's house-design data files; once pieces are
    registered, non-GM placement is restricted to them.

NOTES - Verified non-gaps (no change needed):
  - Design packet streaming already exists: PacketHouseDesignDetailed (0xD8
    multi-plane stream, ClassicUO-parse verified) is SendStructureTo and
    PacketHouseDesignVersion (0xBF 0x1D) is SendVersionTo. The stream splits
    planes by tile count in mode 0 rather than by Z, which the client parses
    correctly.

    DELHOUSE/DELSHIP unregister one regardless of kind, and HOUSES/SHIPS
    report the counts. A uid is only ever a house or a ship, never both.

[2026-07-12] - Sub-90 parity backlog, third batch

ADDED - Account IP-block scheduling:

    relative to Source-X (which inserts each value at the front). For a
    non-default LEVELMAX this mis-assigned the candle requirement per level
    (e.g. LEVELMAX 7 gave [3,2,2,3,3,3] instead of [3,3,3,3,2,2]).

[2026-07-12] - Script FILE object parity with Source-X (CSFileObj)
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - The script FILE object now matches Source-X CSFileObj semantics:
  - Default MODE is append+read+write (was read-only), so a bare FILE.OPEN
    followed by FILE.WRITELINE appends instead of silently no-opping.
  - OPEN is refused while a file is already open; MODE changes are refused
    while open (both logged through the diagnostic sink); CREATE and APPEND
    clear each other like upstream.
  - READCHAR returns the numeric byte value; READBYTE <n> reads n bytes as
    text; both guard reads past EOF. READLINE restores the pre-read POSITION
    (non-destructive) and trims trailing non-graphic characters.
  - LENGTH returns -1 when closed; FILEPATH returns the full resolved path.
  - FILEEXIST/FILELINES/DELETEFILE resolve against the sandbox root instead
    of the open file's directory (previously failed with no file open);
    DELETEFILE refuses the currently-open file.

ADDED - Server-global FILE surface:
  - Scripts running WITHOUT a client console (server hooks, NPC triggers)
    now reach the full FILE surface through the shared server handle
    (Source-X g_Serv._hFile model) — previously only FILE.FILEEXIST worked
    there. The interpreter routes FILE.* verbs to the host as a no-console
    fallback; client consoles keep their existing path.
  - Sandbox unchanged: everything stays under <scpdir>/files with traversal
    and reparse-point rejection (deliberate hardening over Source-X).
  - CSFileObjContainer (multi-file pool) is intentionally not ported: it is
    not wired to the FILE. reference in Source-X either.

[2026-07-11] - Source-X verb long tail completed (48 deferred verbs, backlog now empty)
----------------------------------------

  - GOAWAKE/GOSLEEP flip the object's tick-sleep state; EFFECTLOCATION sends

    already existed).
  - GM tools: NUKE/NUKECHAR (optional verb line applied instead of deleting),
    NUDGE (dx dy dz args), TILE (two-corner flood with cycling item ids),
    EXTRACT/UNEXTRACT (multi text files, version 6 format, sandboxed under
    the script database root), LINK (two-click item cross-link with the key
    lock-uid special case), REPAIR, EVERBTARG (prompt then verb on the last
    target), GOTARG/LAST (last-picked-target memory), BADSPAWN (teleport to a
    spawner whose resource no longer resolves), EDIT (property editor).

ADDED - Server verbs:
  - SERV.BLOCKIP/UNBLOCKIP reachable from scripts behind a PLEVEL_Admin gate
    (srcUid protocol); SERV.CALCCRYPT ports the CCryptoKeyCalc login-key
    derivation and returns/prints the SphereCrypt.ini-style line.

CHANGED:
  - The Source-X verb inventory guardrail's deferred backlog is now EMPTY —
    every pinned CObjBase/CChar/CItem/CClient/CServer verb has an
    implementation site.

[2026-07-11] - Script reading parity, second audit pass (adversarial re-verification)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Lexer:
  - Source-X Str_Parse rule restored: a WHITESPACE key/value separator consumes
    one following separator char, so "name = value" no longer leaks the '=' into
    the value. This recovered 81 numeric [DEFNAME] constants in the reference
    pack (brain_*, LOGL_*, RES_* tables) that silently parsed as text.
  - Source-X GetArgStr quote semantics ported (ScriptKey.StripQuotePair): the
    script runtime strips a surrounding quote pair from verb/property values
    (TAG.X="a b", SYSMESSAGE="msg"), and DEFNAME/GLOBALS/LIST loaders store
    de-quoted values — quoted numerics parse as numbers again.
  - Dialog gump position line ("5,25") and classic MENU titles read the raw
    line; the comma separator had collapsed them (dialogs anchored at 0,0).

FIXED - Expressions:
  - Leading-zero hex now sign-extends like Source-X GetSingle: <=8 significant
    nibbles reinterpret as int32 ("0ffffffff" = -1), 9-16 as int64, more
    overflows to -1; decimal overflow warns and yields -1.
  - QVAL: '?'/':' split skips <...> spans so nested <QVAL ...> works, and the
    numeric form accepts 3-4 args with 0 defaults (was requiring all 5).
  - STR*/MULDIV/BETWEEN/SETBIT-family intrinsics split their argument lists on
    the RAW text (bracket-aware) before resolution — a resolved value
    containing commas ("1,2" coordinates) no longer corrupts the split; also
    fixed STRCMPI's off-by-one prefix slice.
  - Conditional splitter: an unmatched '<'+letter (no-space less-than,
    "IF a<b || c") no longer swallows the rest of the condition.

FIXED - Resource loading:
  - Duplicate script files dedup by file TITLE (basename) like Source-X
    FindResourceFile; directory expansion sorts case-sensitively by filename
    like AddResourceDir.
  - A second [LIST name] block appends to the existing list (AddList reuse).
  - [TYPEDEFS] values are also exposed through the DEF text table so
    <DEF.t_xxx> and numeric resolvers see bulk-declared type names.
  - [NOTOTITLES] threshold lines accept '=' as a separator; the [GLOBALS]
    legacy "VAR." prefix strip is case-sensitive like Source-X.

Known deliberate deviations from Source-X (documented): 0x-prefix hex is
accepted (Source-X yields 0), RAND(hi,lo) normalizes the range, the <...>
separator suppression in key parsing is kept (Source-X computes but ignores
angle depth), and the anywhere-match "VAR." strstr bug is not replicated.

[2026-07-11] - Script reading parity with Source-X (sections, lexer, expressions)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Section types that were previously ignored or unknown now load:
  - [GLOBALS]/[WORLDVARS] and [LIST name]/[WORLDLISTS] script sections seed the
    world's global VARs and LISTs at boot (world save still overrides).
  - [OBSCENE] word list loads and backs a real ISOBSCENE intrinsic
    (Source-X-style *word* wildcard matching); it previously always returned 0.
  - [FAME]/[KARMA] title lists and [NOTOTITLES] (karma/fame thresholds plus the
    (k+1)*(f+1) title matrix with male,female split) load with a
    GetNotoTitle(karma, fame, female) accessor.
  - [RUNES] letter table loads; spell RUNES letter abbreviations ("IPY") now
    decode into real power words through it instead of a hardcoded fallback.
  - [BOOK name page] sections are retained with per-page access; [MENU],
    [SCROLL] and [TIP] keys are retained as well.
  - [TYPEDEFS] bulk declarations register type-name defnames.
  - [RESOURCES] sections inside ANY script file queue extra files for loading
    (Source-X AddResourceFile order: appended after the manifest), with
    spheretables refusal, .scp extension append, root guard and dedup.
  - spheretables.scp: ALL [RESOURCES] sections are processed (not just the
    first), and unlisted top-level *.scp files load afterwards like Source-X
    AddResourceDir.
  - CHAMPION/SPHERECRYPT/KRDIALOGLIST/ACCOUNT/GMPAGE/SECTOR/WORLDCHAR/WORLDITEM/
    WC/WI/WORLDSCRIPT/WS/TIMERF/STAT are recognized (no more Unknown warnings).

CHANGED - Expression evaluation now matches Sphere semantics:
  - Expressions fold right-to-left with NO operator precedence (Source-X
    GetVal/GetValMath): "2*3+1" is 2*(3+1)=8. Old packs rely on this.
  - IF/ELIF/WHILE conditions split at top-level || and && with equal precedence
    and left-to-right short-circuiting (Source-X GetConditionalSubexpressions),
    including !(...) negation and parenthesized recursion.
  - Divide/modulo by zero keeps the left operand (was 0) and logs.
  - SIN/COS/TAN use radians with truncation (was degrees x1000);
    ARCSIN/ARCCOS/ARCTAN and STRASCII added; STRINDEXOF is case-sensitive;
    ID() masks to the low 20 index bits; RAND supports 64-bit ranges; RANDBELL
    is the deterministic Source-X log curve; resolver depth cap raised to 128.
  - Number literals follow Source-X dot rules: leading "0" not followed by '.'
    is hex; dots inside decimals are grouping separators ("100.000"=100000).
  - Weighted {v w ...} ranges reject odd token counts (error, 0) and log
    non-positive weights.
  - <...> references in a numeric context dispatch through the full variable
    resolver (previously <EVAL ...>/<TAG.X> evaluated to 0 there).

CHANGED - Script lexer parity (Source-X Str_Parse):
  - Key/value separator set is now "=, \t" (comma included) with double-quote
    awareness and {} [] () <> depth tracking.
  - ScriptKey.RawLine preserves the verbatim line; raw-line consumers (dialog
    TEXT, [TELEPORTERS], [STARTS], [MOONGATES], [NAMES], title lists) read it,
    fixing multi-word/comma entries that the Key/Arg split used to mangle.
  - FLOAT.-namespace compound assignment rewrites through <FLOATVAL ...>;
    the operator set now includes '!'; section headers accept '=' and ','
    separators ("[ITEMDEF=i_x]").

[2026-07-11] - Source-X script pack, load ordering and runtime compatibility transition
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - Source-X resource loading and text encoding:
  - SCPFILES now points directly to oldSphere/Scripts-X-main. The
    spheretables.scp RESOURCES order loads exactly 756 active files; commented
    and not_complete sources are no longer pulled in by a recursive scan.
  - The script reader supports AUTO, UTF8 and LEGACY modes. AUTO validates strict
    UTF-8 first and falls back to a configurable legacy code page only for an
    invalid UTF-8 stream. SCRIPTENCODING and SCRIPTLEGACYCODEPAGE are available
    in sphere.ini.
  - UTF-8 BOM, Windows-1252 and Turkish Windows-1254 paths are covered by
    regressions, and changing the encoding configuration clears stale file cache.

FIXED - Definitions, PLEVEL and Source-X hook lifecycle:
  - Static ITEMDEF/TEMPLATE loading stops at the first ON=@ trigger body, so
    runtime NAME, TYPE and DISPID statements cannot mutate the shared base def.
  - Every PLEVEL block for the same level is merged across files, preserving the
    complete Source-X command privilege table.
  - Server start/exit/save/save_ok/save_fail/save_finished, resync, TimerCall,
    IP block, connect-request and connection-acquired hooks are wired to their
    real lifecycle events. Save vetoes and non-boolean hook results are retained.
  - Character creation now follows f_onchar_create_init/f_onchar_create and
    passes client feature flags, profession and race through trigger arguments;
    cancellation leaves no partial character record.

ADDED - SERV and global script surface:
  - SERV.SPELL, extended ITEMDEF fields, combat/magic/option flags, SCPFILES,
    decay, housing, NPC training and guild/town stone lookups are available.
  - SERV.NEWITEM and SERV.NEWNPC work as client-independent global factories,
    retaining NEW references and core definition state.
  - DB, LDB and MDB commands/row lookups work from server hooks; MDB.IMPORTDB and
    FILE.FILEEXIST support the Source-X startup functions.
  - Unknown ITEMDEF fields remain diagnostic-visible while also being retained
    as extended definition properties for runtime and SERV queries.

FIXED - DIALOG, SPEECH and EVENTS script compatibility:
  - DIALOG layout lines run through the shared script interpreter, allowing gump
    commands produced by functions, CALL/RETURN and conditional control flow.
    BUTTONTILEART, XMFHTMLTOK, ITEMPROPERTY and PICINPIC are supported.
  - SPEECH matching supports embedded *, ?, character ranges and legacy <ANY>
    patterns. NPC, item and MULTIDEF TSPEECH/SPEECH chains retain the speaking
    client's script context and run from their actual event points.
  - HouseDesignBegin, AddMulti and NPCSeeWantItem fire from native gameplay
    flows; the legacy @ItemUnEquipTest spelling is compatible with @ItemUnequip.
  - Scripted ITEMDEF identity and metadata application is centralized across
    item creation paths. TEVENTS is distinct from dynamic EVENTS and legacy
    saves cannot execute the same handler twice.

FIXED - Deep parser, definition and script-verb compatibility:
  - NPC skills written as 15.0/100.0 are converted to the runtime tenths scale;
    the script parser supports *=, /= and %= assignments.
  - ITEMDEF CAN, CANUSE, LAYER and TDATA1-4 plus CHARDEF SOUND, DEFNAME2,
    FOODTYPE, COLOR, ERA and AOS resistance fields load symbolic DEFNAME values
    and forward references without losing their identity. Named ITEMDEF runtime
    metadata no longer collapses to the 16-bit client graphic id during lookups.
  - ADDCLILOC, ADDCONTEXTENTRY, PROMPTCONSOLE/U, SPELLEFFECT, NOTOUPDATE/CLEAR,
    CHANGEFACE, SERV.DELETEFILE and SERV.CONSOLE are wired to operational client
    and server paths. Enhanced Client face selection uses Source-X gump context
    0x2B0.
  - Unterminated SCP section headers emit file-and-line diagnostics and tolerate
    the missing closing bracket, preserving the affected resource body.

VERIFIED - The real Scripts-X-main manifest parses all 756 declared files and
  builds the definition registries. The complete solution, including Source-X
  smoke/regression coverage, passes 1355/1355 with zero build warnings/errors.

[2026-07-10] - General gameplay integrity: inventory, trade, social systems and world lifecycle
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Items, containers, weight and object lifecycle:
  - Container cycles, duplicate parent/equipment references, deep stack weight
    and full pack/container operations are safe. Bank, vendor and special service
    layers no longer count toward carried weight.
  - Deleted items and characters are removed from the object table, sectors,
    equipment and complete child-container trees together. Stale references can
    no longer delete recycled UIDs, and consumed objects leave no ghost records.
  - Death, corpses, resurrection, NPC looting, crafting, script DUPE/CONT/BOUNCE,
    stack splitting and drag/drop paths restore or ground items instead of losing
    them when a destination reaches capacity.

FIXED - Vendors, banking and secure trade:
  - Duplicate vendor rows cannot exceed stock; malformed BUY templates no longer
    accept everything; transient clones are removed; full-pack purchases safely
    fall back to the ground. Stock, payment and payout state stays world-consistent.
  - Bank withdrawals and check creation now guarantee delivery before deducting
    the balance, so capacity or carry failures cannot consume banked gold.
  - Secure trade enforces target eligibility, REFUSETRADES, TradeCreate/DropOn
    triggers, incoming weight and slot limits, returning every item safely after
    cancellation or failed completion.

FIXED - Party, guild, pet and mount behavior:
  - Party invitations enforce leader authority, a 120-second timeout, membership
    and capacity checks. Forged private party messages and destructive force-add
    attempts are rejected.
  - Guild candidate/member/master privileges are distinct. Master election,
    server-side gump authorization, fealty, guild/alliance chat, mirrored war and
    alliance relations and legacy save repair now follow Source-X behavior.
  - Wild and foreign mounts cannot be ridden, while Mount/Dismount triggers veto
    before mutation. Stable and figurine restore failures preserve both pets and
    items when follower limits or destinations are invalid.

FIXED - Magic, travel, scripts and client interactions:
  - Recall, teleport, summon, field and NEWDUPE operations validate map/sector
    bounds; failed placement leaves no orphan object or ownership state.
  - Loaded active spell effects validate duration and flags. Consumed scrolls,
    potions, bandages, bulletin posts and trade containers fully leave the world.
  - Script/GM item placement, legacy figurine ownership, container capacity and
    complete stack state/attribute cloning no longer lose or corrupt data.

  solution passes 1328/1328 in Debug and Release. The git diff check is clean.

  - Pilot/wheel control requires the assigned pilot to be aboard, unmounted,

FIXED - Persistence and reload safety:
  - House/ship regions, owners, components, direction, storage and pilot data are

[2026-07-10] - Deep combat code audit: swings, ranged combat, damage and kill credit
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Swing state and combat safety:
  - Pending swings are cleared on target changes, war-mode exit, death, deletion
    and resurrection. Map, life state, immunity, region, LOS and range are
    revalidated at hit time; weapon/range/Recoil_NoRange are committed at windup.
  - NPC and player HitCheck paths now use the same ordering and callback data.
    CHARDEF innate range, ITEMDEF melee range, NoDirChange, Reveal and owner crime
    reporting now match Source-X behavior.

FIXED - Ranged weapons and ammunition economy:
  - Ammunition is found recursively in nested containers with depth/cycle guards;
    ammo lost during windup cannot produce a free hit. StayInRange misses execute
    HitMiss, projectile, Arrow and player-ammunition handling completely.
  - Full-container stuck-ammo merging/orphan cleanup and NPC HitMiss weapon/Arrow
    UID callback data are corrected. A full parry is no longer treated as a miss
    and cannot incorrectly trigger ammunition economy.

FIXED - Damage, armor, speed and durability:
  - Miss, parry and proc-resolved outcomes are distinct; trigger cancellation
    always stops damage regardless of callback return value. A proc kill prevents
    the original strike from being applied again.
  - Armor-layer coverage, resist/slayer/AOS bonuses, the elemental Source-X
    formula, weapon damage overrides and ITEMDEF SKILL support are corrected;
    overflow and double-roll durability errors are removed.
  - Source-X swing-speed eras 0-2 are implemented. Invented mounted/two-handed
    penalties are removed, SPEEDSCALEFACTOR is bound to config/script and SSI
    aggregation is overflow-safe.

FIXED - Crime, combat memory and death credit:
  - CombatStart runs before mutations with the target as SRC and repeated attacks
    are idempotent. Aggressor/HarmedBy directions, memory expiry/death cleanup and
    attacker damage overflow/negative-kill handling are corrected.
  - When no final killer is supplied, the strongest logged attacker is used. One
    attacker's cancelled Kill callback no longer blocks other credits and the
    attacker list is cleared after distribution.

[2026-07-10] - Infrastructure hardening: IPC, panel lifecycle, paths and CI
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Managed Host/Server IPC now reports truthful results:
  - Mutation failures and remote exceptions are no longer converted into
    success. Responses carry structured error codes and the panel maps
    unavailable, timeout and rejected operations to 503/504/502.
  - Requests are serialized and every live-world/account operation is
    marshalled onto the game main loop instead of entering state concurrently
    from pipe threads.
  - Disconnect, restart and shutdown now cancel and join their background
    work; stale connection retries cannot interfere with a newer server.

SECURITY - File access is contained under trusted roots:
  - Script, database, world-operation and panel paths share one relative-path
    resolver that rejects absolute paths, traversal, sibling-prefix escapes
    and reparse/symlink descendants.
  - Panel script writes are atomic, backups are collision-safe, uploads have
    size limits and ZIP extraction uses the same containment checks.

FIXED - Panel sessions and API behavior:
  - Logout sends the original bearer token before clearing local state, so the
    server can actually revoke it. Expired tokens are removed and purged.
  - Setup configuration is public only during first-run setup; account/debug/
    lifecycle endpoints preserve backend false results and return meaningful
    HTTP failures instead of silent success.

CHANGED - Reproducible quality gates:
  - Axios/Vite and transitive dependencies were updated; npm audit reports no
    known vulnerabilities. ESLint and Vitest were added for the Vue panel.
  - CI now runs npm ci, lint, panel tests, dependency audit, production build,
    Debug/Release .NET builds, all tests and coverage collection.
  - Empty duplicate test projects were removed. Infrastructure regressions
    cover path containment, IPC serialization/results, tokens and panel HTTP
    statuses. A flaky adjacent-tactician test now restores its own precondition.

VERIFIED - Debug and Release build with zero warnings/errors; 1217 .NET tests
  and 2 panel tests pass. Current coverage is 45.93% lines / 36.98% branches.

  gates, 3/4-sight cap, exact dice), breath dist>=1 + unclamped
  BREATH.DAM tag, wand HAND1-only, ally-heal only for allies fighting
  the same enemy, target stickiness +8, berserk distance preference,
  hidden-NPC ambush, mid-fight target rescan only under multi-attacker
  pressure, obstacle TopZ window, guard yells per new target, vendor
  restock honors RESTOCKVENDORS/NORESTOCK region tags, pet GO resumes
  the previous order, @NPCActFollow RETURN 1 stops following.

================================================================================
[2026-07-04] - 56T spawner import: every def-typed spawner came up dead
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Imported legacy spawners never spawned (56T field report):
  - Item defname resolution returned 0 for any itemdef without an ID
    override (DispIndex 0 short-circuited the fallback), so every
    i_worldgem_bit imported with BaseId 0.
  - InitializeSpawnComponent gated on the raw TYPE field; Sphere saves
    omit TYPE when it matches the base itemdef, so def-typed spawners
    silently no-opped. It now gates on the virtualized item type.
  - MORE1=c_xxx (a raw chardef defname in legacy saves) fell through the
    ItemDef-gated resolver; the parked MORE1_DEFNAME tag is now consumed
    for both NPC and item spawners.
  - The world bootstrap no longer clobbers an explicitly saved TYPE with
    the itemdef type, and it initializes item spawners (t_spawn_item)
    which were skipped entirely.
  - Real-data test: 2660 NPC + 53 item spawners from C:\56T\save now
    import alive (1 dead worldgem is the shard's own MORE1=00 quirk).

CHANGED - NpcAI.cs decomposed into concern-based partial classes
  (Core/Combat/Magic/Movement/Perception/TownRoles/Pet), no behavior
  change.

================================================================================
[2026-07-03] - Field-report wave 2: ridden-mount targeting, door auto-close
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Monsters could target a ridden mount:
  - IsAttackable never skipped STATF_RIDDEN, so a hostile locked onto
    the mount under a rider and started an invisible one-sided fight
    (the ridden NPC skips its AI tick, so it could never respond).
    Attacks now go to the RIDER.

ADDED - Door auto-close (Source-X _SetTimeoutS(20) parity):
  - An opened door swings shut on its own after 20 seconds: the art
    flips back, the hinge shift is undone, the close sound plays and
    the visual is pushed to observers. A manual close cancels the timer.

VERIFIED - The pathfinder shares MapDataManager.IsPassable, so the
  mountain-walk fix covers A* routing as well as direct steps.

================================================================================
[2026-07-03] - Field-report wave: door hinge shift, pet self-defense, mountain walk, 56T saves
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Doors appeared to open backwards:
  - Opening only flipped the art +1; the Source-X Use_Door HINGE SHIFT
    (per 0-15 door-set slot) was never applied, so the open art rendered
    anchored at the wrong tile. The reference door-base table is ported
    verbatim (declaration order, overlap quirks); player, NPC and
    map-static door paths all move the leaf now. The map-static path
    also restored the wrong closing art (tileId-1 below the closed art).

FIXED - A following/staying pet never defended itself:
  - Follow/Come/Stay never read FightTarget, so an attacked pet just
    stood there. Pets now fight back (Source-X Memory_FightStart);
    follow/come/stay/stop orders call the pet off.

FIXED - NPCs walked over mountains:
  - IsPassable only checked land for water; the land IMPASSABLE flag
    (mountain rock) was never consulted, and each slope step passes the
    +-12 z gate on its own. Impassable land now blocks unless a
    surface/bridge static covers the spot.

ADDED - Sphere 0.56T save compatibility:
  - A real-data test loads C:\56T\save (76k items, 4.2k chars). Item
    TIMER=seconds now restores the decay/spawn schedule, book AUTHOR
    maps to its tag, DISCORDANCE resolves to the Enticement skill and
    char TIMER (transient AI tick) is accepted. Unknown 56T-custom keys
    stay preserved as SAVE.* tags.

ADDED - In-game world-ops routing:
  - EXPORT/IMPORT/RESTORE/SAVESTATICS/LOAD (already implemented on the
    script surface) are now reachable from .serv.* in game.

ADDED - The NEWNPC script verb (Source-X SSV_NEWNPC):
  - Spawns a chardef NPC through the full GM-add pipeline (@Create, brain
    finalisation, @CreateLoot, appearance broadcast) at the invoker's
    feet, reachable as SERV.LASTNEWCHAR. RECALL was closed by research:
    it is not a char verb in Source-X either (only the spell).

CHANGED - Ghost manifest now keys off STATF_INSUBSTANTIAL (Source-X):
  - A fresh ghost is born insubstantial; the war toggle while dead flips
    the flag (war = manifest); resurrection clears it; the view filter
    reads the flag (war-mode fallback for pre-existing saves). Scripts
    now see and can set the same bit as the reference.

[2026-07-03] - Housing wave H1b: house placement footprint validation
----------------------------------------

FIXED - House placement validation gaps (Source-X Multi_Create loop):
  - NOBUILDING is now checked across the footprint plus a +5-tile margin
    (previously only the single anchor point).
  - A docked ship hull under the footprint blocks placement (new ship
    engine hook); blocking ground items (ITEMDEF I_Block) reject cells.
  - The living-character check was silently a no-op (a range-0 scan

[2026-07-03] - Housing/ship wave H1: redeed cargo crate, REDEED teardown, placement overlap
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Ship redeed deleted the hold cargo:
  - RemoveShip now moves component contents to a moving crate, delivered
    to the owner's bank box or dropped (with decay) at the ship's spot —
    the Source-X TransferAllItemsToMovingCrate behavior ships lacked.

FIXED - The REDEED verb leaked the house from the registry:
  - It called house.Redeed directly, leaving a stale registry entry (a
    burned house-count slot) and a ghost dynamic region. The verb now
    routes through the housing engine's full teardown.

FIXED - Ship placement did not check hull overlap:
  - CanPlaceShip only verified water; two ships (or a ship over a hull)
    could be spawned overlapping. The footprint now rejects any cell
    already covered by another ship.

[2026-07-03] - Movement wave M1: map edge-case crash fixes
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Negative coordinates slipped past the sector bounds guard:
  - Truncating integer division resolved X/Y in [-63,-1] to sector 0, so
    off-map placements/moves/teleports were accepted and the map readers
    then crashed on a negative cell index. GetSector now rejects the
    negative side explicitly.

FIXED - Pathfinder explored off-map neighbor tiles:
  - An NPC pathfinding from the x=0 / y=0 map edge passed -1 into the
    map readers (crash reachable by ordinary NPC AI); the far edge read
    garbage cells. Neighbors are now bounds-checked against the map size.

FIXED - The GM/AllMove/CanPassWalls walk bypass could step off the map;
  the bypass branch now validates the target sector too.

[2026-07-03] - Death/corpse wave D3: kill record, corpse hair, antimagic rez, summon burst
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Kill record (Source-X LOGM_KILLS + party echo):
  - A player death logs "'<victim>' was killed by 'A', 'B'." (or
    "accident.") and echoes the line to the victim's party members.

ADDED - Corpses render hair and beard:
  - Hair/beard are copied onto the corpse as marked render dupes
    (Source-X CreateDupeItem); the originals stay on the ghost and the
    dupes are discarded on corpse rejoin instead of restoring as loot.

ADDED - Antimagic resurrection gate:
  - A NoMagic region refuses the resurrection (Source-X
    REGION_ANTIMAGIC_ALL); a GM ghost bypasses.

ADDED - Corpseless summon death bursts the spell-fizzle effect (0x3735)
  instead of silently vanishing (Source-X MakeCorpse).

  max-weight anti-exploit (no container weight-capacity model exists to
  hook), blessed-items-to-pack (deliberate feel choice), the dead-season/
