[2026-06-30] - Multi parity: ship ban / eject bound to the ship region (Wave 177)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Ship ban / eject (Source-X multi ban list, enforced through the ship region):
  - A ship now carries a ban list. Boarding is gated through the ship's dynamic
    region: a movement onto any tile resolved (region-bound) to a ship the mover is
    banned from is refused, exactly like the house ban gate. The owner is never
    barred.
  - Banning a player who is currently on deck ejects them — they are put on the tile
    just beyond the hull's starboard edge (this move fires region enter/exit normally
    since they really are leaving the ship), and the boarding gate then keeps them
    off.
  - Ship lookup is region-bound: FindShipAt resolves the ship via the Ship-flag
    region under a tile, so deck membership matches the footprint the engine already
    maintains rather than a separate bounding-box test.
  - Ban lists persist across save / load (SHIP.BANS tag).

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Multi parity: dynamic ship region tracking the hull as it sails (Wave 176)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Ship region model (Source-X CItemMulti::MultiRealizeRegion + CRegionWorld move):
  - A ship now realizes a dynamic world region matching its hull footprint, flagged
    Ship and inheriting the surrounding region's flags (a guarded harbour / no-pvp
    sea carries through, with Ship added). Created on placement and on load, torn
    down on dry-dock. Being the smallest-area region over the footprint, FindRegion
    resolves to it on deck, so Ship-flag and region-flag-dependent systems apply
    aboard.
  - Unlike a house, the ship MOVES, so the region is re-positioned to the new
    footprint after every move and turn, and its inherited flags are RECOMPUTED
    (reset to base, re-inherit from the region the hull now sits in) rather than
    accumulated — a ship sailing out of a guarded zone correctly loses Guarded.
  - The ship's @RegionLeave / @RegionEnter boundary check now resolves the
    BACKGROUND region the hull sits in (excluding the ship's own region, which would
    otherwise win FindRegion by smallest area), so crossing a sea / harbour boundary
    still fires.
  - Deck characters carried by a moving / turning ship no longer fire region
    enter/exit or flip CURRENT_REGION: the region travels with the hull, so they are
    not crossing a boundary (new MoveCharacter fireRegionEvents=false path).

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Multi parity: house footprint region, leading-edge ship collision, placement Z-flatness (Wave 175)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Housing region model (Source-X CItemMulti::MultiRealizeRegion):
  - A placed house now realizes a dynamic world region matching its footprint,
    flagged House and inheriting the containing region's flags (a guarded / no-pvp /
    safe town carries through, with House added). Being the smallest-area region over
    the footprint, FindRegion resolves to it inside the house, so House-flag and
    region-flag-dependent systems now apply indoors. The region is created on
    placement and on load, and torn down on collapse / redeed. Houses are static so
    the region never needs to track movement. (Ship regions remain a separate phase.)

FIXED - Ship movement collision (Source-X CCMultiMovable::Move):
  - A moving ship now tests only the LEADING EDGE in the move direction (both
    perpendicular edges for a diagonal) for water, instead of re-scanning its whole
    footprint. The cells the ship already occupies are water by definition; testing
    them again was redundant. Behaviour is unchanged for solid water but matches the
    engine's edge-scan model and is the basis for future deck-object collection.

FIXED - House placement Z-flatness (Source-X CItemMulti::Multi_Create):
  - House placement now rejects a footprint cell whose surface Z differs from the
    placement Z by more than 4, so a house can no longer straddle a slope or cliff.
    Guarded by map data being loaded (no effect in headless / no-MUL runs).

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Ship/housing parity: turn preflight, collapse moving-crate, deed targeting, @HouseCheck (Wave 174)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Ship:
  - Turning a ship now preflights the new facing's footprint and ABORTS before any
    mutation if it would not fit (water/passable), instead of swapping the BaseId
    and rotating all components / deck characters / items with no fit check and no
    rollback — which could leave a ship half-rotated onto land. Magic ships still
    turn anywhere.

FIXED - Housing:
  - A collapsing house no longer scatters its locked-down / secured items on the
    ground to decay (item loss). They are reparented into a MOVING CRATE — a
    secured container moves whole — and the crate is delivered to the owner's bank
    box (fallback: the house tile). Reparenting, not copying, so no dupe.

ADDED - Housing:
  - House deeds now ask for a TARGET tile (Source-X) and place the house there,
    instead of dropping it at the player's feet on double-click.
  - @HouseCheck script hook: a script may veto house placement (RETURN 1) after the
    engine's NoBuild / footprint / terrain checks pass; ARGN1/2/3 = x/y/z.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Region parity: InheritParent flag/tag/event inheritance (Wave 173)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Region nesting (Source-X REGION_FLAG_INHERIT_PARENT_*):
  - A region flagged InheritParentFlags / InheritParentTags / InheritParentEvents
    now pulls the corresponding state from its containing parent region at load.
    The "parent" is the smallest region with a larger area that contains the
    region's representative point (P=, or the centre of its first rect). Inheritance
    is additive (the region keeps its own flags/tags/events) and the inherit-control
    bits themselves are not propagated. Runs once after all AREADEFs load.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Region/spawn parity: NoMining, anti-magic sub-flags, underground light, item-spawn timing (Wave 172)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Region flag behaviours (Source-X REGION_*):
  - NoMining (REGION_FLAG_NOMINING): mining is refused in the region.
  - Anti-magic sub-flags now enforced: RecallOut blocks recalling out, the Recall
    flag blocks recalling/gating IN, the Gate flag blocks gate travel, NoTeleport
    blocks teleporting into the region, and NoMagicDamage fizzles harmful spells.
    The legacy numeric region properties (RECALLOUT/RECALLIN/GATEOUT/GATEIN = 0)
    keep working alongside the flags.

FIXED:
  - Underground light no longer clobbered: the periodic global-light broadcast now
    skips clients standing in an Underground (dungeon) region, so a player in a
    dungeon keeps the fixed dungeon light instead of suddenly seeing surface
    daylight on the next light tick. Surface light is restored on region exit.
  - Item spawners (IT_SPAWN_ITEM) now honour TIMELO/TIMEHI (respawn interval, in
    minutes) and MAXDIST (scatter range) like the char spawner — and fixed a
    latent bug where these properties were stored as tags but never applied to the
    spawn component (affecting char spawners too).
  - Sector.Number is computed from the map's true column count (width / 64)
    instead of a hardcoded 96, so it is correct on non-6144-wide maps.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - NPC AI parity: wand casting (Wave 171)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - NPC AI:
  - A casting NPC holding a charged wand (IT_WAND with a spell id in More1 and a
    CHARGES tag) now throws the wand's spell ~50% of the time (Source-X
    NPC_FightMagery wand source). The wand path is mana-free and bypasses the book
    mana gates, so it fires even when the NPC is low on mana — and a wand-only NPC
    with no spellbook can cast from it. Each wand cast consumes a charge; at zero
    the wand's spell clears (mirroring the player double-click wand path). A wand
    with no CHARGES tag is treated as infinite. Additive — only NPCs with an
    equipped wand are affected.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - NPC AI parity: config heal threshold, @NPCActFight skip-hardcoded, @NPCActCast target (Wave 170)
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - NPC AI:
  - A casting NPC's self-heal decision now uses the configured wound threshold
    (NPCHEALTHRESHOLD, default 30%) instead of a hardcoded 50% (Source-X
    NPC_FightCast iHealThreshold); below half the threshold it prefers GreaterHeal.

ADDED - NPC AI triggers:
  - @NPCActFight LOCAL.skiphardcoded = 1 makes the engine bypass its hardcoded
    breath / throw specials while keeping flee / magery / melee (Source-X
    fSkipHardcoded), distinct from RETURN 1 which suppresses the whole action.
  - @NPCActCast LOCAL.target = a uid redirects the cast onto a different target
    (Source-X REF1 target override), in addition to the existing ARGN1 spell
    override and RETURN 1 abort.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Attack-as-crime tied to personal notoriety (self-defense) (Wave 169)
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - Attack / spell as crime (Source-X CCharFight NOTO_GOOD):
  - Attacking is a crime only when the target is NOTO_GOOD (innocent blue) FROM
    THE ATTACKER'S OWN VIEW. Because personal grey now folds in the attacker's
    SawCrime / HarmedBy memory, retaliating against an aggressor who struck first
    — or against someone whose crime the attacker witnessed — is self-defense and
    no longer flags the defender criminal. A globally criminal / murderer /
    guild / party target is likewise not NOTO_GOOD. The aggressor and victim still
    record their IAggressor / HarmedBy memory, and attacking a true innocent in a
    guarded region still flags the aggressor.
  - The same personal-view rule now gates the harmful-spell crime: a spell on a
    target the caster holds SawCrime / HarmedBy of is self-defense, not a crime.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Crime/notoriety parity: CheckCrimeSeen witness pipeline, fame/karma split (Wave 168)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Crime witness pipeline (Source-X CChar::CheckCrimeSeen):
  - When a crime is committed, every character in view range with line of sight —
    and, for a covert crime, the winner of the perception skill contest (the
    viewer's vs the criminal's skill) — notices it: the witness records a per-
    viewer MEMORY_SAWCRIME (so the criminal shows grey to THEM via personal grey),
    a guarded-region NPC witness calls the guards (global criminal flag), and
    @SeeCrime / @SeeSnoop fire so a script can react or escalate. A crime no one
    sees has no consequence.
  - Stealing and snooping now run this witness pipeline instead of the old blind
    50% / config-toggle MakeCriminal: an unseen theft is consequence-free, a
    witnessed one makes the thief grey to the witnesses (and globally criminal in
    a guarded area). Snooping respects the snoop-criminal chance.
  - Personal grey now also keys on MEMORY_SAWCRIME (in addition to the aggressor
    HarmedBy memory), matching Source-X Noto_CalcFlag's SAWCRIME | AGGREIVED.
  - New @SeeSnoop character trigger.

CHANGED - Death credit (Source-X Noto_Kill):
  - Fame, karma and experience on a kill are now divided across every damaging
    attacker (iTotalKillers), so a group splits the spoils instead of the final
    blow taking all of it. A solo kill is unchanged.
  - Killing a criminal / red now yields NO karma — the would-be loss is clamped
    to 0 and no positive karma is awarded (previously a criminal victim's negative
    karma granted the killer a small positive gain).

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Notoriety display parity: personal-grey, pet-inherits-owner, @Criminal duration (Wave 167)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Notoriety display:
  - Personal grey (Source-X aggressor memory): a player who harmed the viewer —
    an active aggressor such as a wilderness attacker who is not globally criminal
    — now shows grey to THAT viewer while the fight memory lasts, so a victim can
    see who is attacking them. The innocent victim stays blue to the aggressor.
    Display-only; it does not change attack-crime legality.
  - A tamed pet / summon now inherits its owner's notoriety colour (Source-X
    Noto_GetFlag pet->owner): the viewer's own pet shows friendly green, another
    player's pet takes that owner's colour, and an ownerless creature falls back
    to its NPC notoriety.

ADDED - Triggers:
  - @Criminal can override the criminal-flag duration via ARGN1 (seconds);
    RETURN 1 still cancels the flag entirely. OnCriminalCheck now returns the
    duration (null = cancel, 0 = engine default).

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Notoriety/crime parity II: multi-attacker murder marking, decay persistence, trigger contract (Wave 166)
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - Murder / crime:
  - A murder is now marked against EVERY unprovoked attacker of an innocent
    player, not just the final-blow killer (Source-X Noto_Kill loops the damage
    list) — ganking an innocent flags the whole group. Each attacker is resolved
    pet->master, deduped, and gated through the same unprovoked-innocent-kill
    check (self-defence / criminal-or-red victims are exempt).
  - The murder-decay countdown is now persisted (MURDERDECAY): a murderer's kill
    count keeps ageing across save/load instead of restarting the full decay
    window on every reload.

ADDED - Triggers:
  - @MurderMark gains an ARGN2 make-criminal toggle: a script can record the
    murder count while suppressing the temporary criminal flag (RETURN 1 still
    blocks the mark + flag entirely).
  - @MurderDecay can read back the seconds until the NEXT decay (ARGN2), letting
    a script override the decay interval per character (0 = engine default).

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Item/inventory parity II: bounce-to-origin, bank deep cap, contained-item reach (Wave 165)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Drop / container:
  - Drag bounce-to-origin (Source-X CClientEvent): a failed drop now returns the
    item to the exact container slot / ground tile it was lifted from, instead of
    dumping it into the backpack. The lift origin is captured at pickup as
    transient per-client state (not item tags, which would break stack-merge
    equality); equip-origin and a gone/full origin fall back to the pack.
  - The bank item cap now counts the WHOLE bank tree (nested bags included), so a
    player can't nest containers to bypass the limit (Source-X deep count). A
    drop anywhere in the bank tree is measured from the bank root.

CHANGED - Use:
  - Double-clicking an item INSIDE a container now verifies reach through the
    container's top parent (Source-X CClientUse), closing a gap where a crafted /
    stale DClick could use an item in a far or moved container. Loose ground
    items keep their existing tile-distance check; GM bypasses.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Item/inventory rule parity: move gate, equip gate, container cap, ground-drop args, decay veto (Wave 164)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Inventory rules:
  - Central ItemMoveRules.CanMove gate (Source-X CChar::CanMoveItem): a frozen or
    dead mover can't lift, and ATTR_MOVE_NEVER items (corpses, static furniture)
    never drag. Wired into the packet pickup path; GM bypasses.
  - Central Character.CanEquip gate (Source-X CChar::CanEquipLayer): validates the
    target layer is a real wearable slot and the wearer meets the item's REQSTR.
    Wired into the player equip path (GM actor bypasses); a per-instance
    OVERRIDE.REQSTR tag overrides the ITEMDEF requirement.
  - Per-container OVERRIDE.MAXITEMS: a container's item cap (e.g. a small pouch, a
    quest box) now overrides the global default when dropping into it.

CHANGED - Drop / decay:
  - @DropOn_Ground now passes the drop point as ARGN1/2/3 (x/y/z) and a DECAY
    local (seconds); a script can relocate the drop (re-validated against map
    bounds + reach) or set a custom rot timer. RETURN 1 still bounces the drop.
  - Item decay now consults @Timer before destruction (Source-X CItem: decay IS
    the item timer). RETURN 1 keeps the item and re-arms a fresh decay window so a
    script can defer/cancel the rot; items with no handler decay as before.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Death/corpse parity III: death shroud, resurrection robe, bonded-pet ghost, death-broadcast centralization (Wave 163)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Death / Resurrection:
  - Death shroud: a Move_Never, Newbie robe is equipped on the ghost's Robe layer
    at death (the real robe has already dropped to the corpse), so the body shows
    the shroud and the player keeps a covering through resurrection. It rides the
    existing ghost appearance broadcast — no separate packet. Gated by the static
    DeathEngine.EnableDeathShroud flag (Source-X CChar::Death).
  - Resurrection robe: when no body covering is restored on resurrection (no
    corpse rejoined, or the corpse held no robe), a plain robe is granted so the
    player is not resurrected naked (Source-X Spell_Resurrection). The shroud is
    stripped first so a robe restored from the corpse can reclaim the Robe layer.

CHANGED - Bonded pets:
  - A bonded pet kept alive server-side as a ghost on death no longer receives the
    0xAF death animation + explicit 0x1D delete broadcast. Those forced the mobile
    off ghost-capable observers (staff / dead / SpiritSpeak) only for the
    view-delta to re-add it the next tick — a flicker. The view-delta now owns the
    bonded pet's appearance: it hides the dead pet from plain players (clean
    vanish) and re-draws it on resurrection. Ordinary NPCs, which are deleted
    server-side, keep their delete broadcast unchanged.

CHANGED - Internal:
  - The corpse broadcast + victim-client ghost transition shared by the three
    server death entry points (spell-kill, lifecycle-kill, GM/AI kill) is folded
    into one BroadcastDeathEffects helper — the player-vs-NPC packet order and the
    bonded-pet gate now live in a single place.

================================================================================

[2026-06-30] - Death/corpse parity II: no-corpse summons, two-stage decay, corpse-rez, @Resurrect args (Wave 162)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Death / Corpse:
  - Summoned creatures and DEATH_NOCORPSE (DEATHFLAGS bit 0x02) leave no corpse —
    they vanish (Source-X MakeCorpse). DEATH_NOLOOTDROP (0x04) makes a corpse but
    keeps the loot off it. Corpses are flagged Move_Never (a corpse is looted, not
    dragged).
  - Player corpses now decay in two stages (Source-X): the first decay turns the
    corpse into a bones pile its owner can no longer rejoin and which keeps its
    contents for a second window; only the second decay scatters the loot. NPC
    corpses are unchanged (single decay, contents deleted).

FIXED - Resurrection:
  - Resurrecting onto a corpse is gated like Source-X FindMyCorpse: the corpse must
    be top-level (not in a container), not flagged NOREJOIN (a decayed bones pile),
    in line of sight, and owned by the resurrecting character.
  - @Resurrect now passes the character's own corpse (ARGO) and the post-rez hit%
    (ARGN1, default 50); a script may override the hit% via ARGN1. RETURN 1 still
    blocks the resurrection.
  - Healing and Veterinary can now target a corpse to resurrect its dead owner
    (Source-X corpse-target Skill_Healing), not only a living character.

FIXED - Tests:
  - Tightened a fishing gathering-test assertion that over-matched an unrelated
    RNG message, removing an intermittent test failure.


----------------------------------------

ADDED - Gathering:
  - Mining requires a pickaxe, lumberjacking an axe, and fishing a fishing pole
    (in hand or pack); the tool wears out and eventually breaks (Source-X). You can
    no longer gather barehanded.
  - A resource node now keeps the resource it rolled on the first strike instead of
    re-rolling (iron→gold) on every swing, and its regen timer no longer starts at
    creation — a partly-mined vein is no longer reset early. The depletion pool is
    stored as a full int.

FIXED - Crafting:
  - Recipe resources can now match by item TYPE (Source-X RES_TYPEDEF — e.g. "any
    ingot"), not just a specific BaseId. A t_* resource used to resolve to a type
    id stored as a bogus BaseId, making the recipe uncraftable; type resources now
    count/consume any item of that type across sub-containers.
  - The crafting menu is paginated (Prev/Next), so recipes past the first screen are
    reachable — long recipe lists were silently cut off at y>390.

FIXED - Smelting / Delivery:
  - Custom ore can smelt to a non-standard ingot via TAG.SMELT_TO (on the ore item
    or its itemdef); standard ore still uses the iron-ingot graphic with the ore
    hue carried over.
  - A gathered/smelted item now drops to the ground when the backpack is full
    instead of being silently lost (the old path "added" it to a full 500-item pack
    — a no-op — then told the client it was there, a desync). Source-X ItemBounce.

[2026-06-30] - Speech/command security + parity: privilege gate, speech cancel, greeting memory (Wave 160)
----------------------------------------

SECURITY - Commands:
  - Setting a property via the command prefix now requires staff privilege
    (Counsel+). A plain player could previously escalate or cheat by typing
    ".GM=1", ".INVUL=1", ".MAGERY=1200", ".STR=5000", ".NAME=...", ".EVENTS=..."
    etc. — the "verb=value" and object-verb fallbacks called TrySetProperty before
    any privilege check (Source-X Event_Command → CanUsePrivVerb). PRIVLEVEL /
    PLEVEL / FLAGS remain unsettable at any level.

FIXED - Speech:
  - A speaker's @Speech self-trigger RETURN 1 now cancels the utterance (Source-X
    Event_Talk): no nearby broadcast and no NPC hear. ProcessSpeech's result was
    previously ignored, so the speech always went out.
  - Being hidden/invisible no longer stops a listener from hearing a whisper
    (Source-X CanHear has no such gate) — a hidden GM still hears.

FIXED - NPC hearing:
  - @NPCHearGreeting now fires only on FIRST contact with a speaker (Source-X
    NPC_OnHear records MEMORY_SPEAK), not on every line. It used to fire each
    utterance, so a RETURN-1 greeting could swallow all of a player's speech and
    the NPC re-greeted endlessly.



FIXED - Smelting:
  - Smelting now carries the ore's hue onto the ingot, so a coloured/special ore
    (valorite, verite, …) produces its matching coloured ingot instead of always
    becoming plain iron (coloured ingots share the iron ingot graphic and differ
    only by hue).

FIXED - Gathering / Triggers:
  - @ResourceTest RETURN 1 now blocks the gather, and @ResourceGather RETURN 1
    cancels the reap; @ResourceGather can also override the reaped item id (ARGN1)
    and amount (ARGN2). Resource triggers now copy the script's ARGN1/2/3 mutations
    back (same mechanism as the char-trigger path) — previously their return value
    and arg changes were ignored.

FIXED - Gathering / Terrain:
  - Fishing now requires a water tile and Lumberjacking a tree at the target
    (Source-X CWorldMap), so you can no longer fish on dry land or chop wood on
    open ground. Mining already validated its tile. The checks stay permissive when
    no map tiledata is loaded.



FIXED - Stable:
  - Claiming a stabled pet no longer loses it when the owner's follower cap is
    full. The pet is only removed from the stable AFTER ownership is successfully
    re-assigned; if the cap check fails the temp NPC is deleted and the pet stays
    stabled (Source-X CCharNPCAct_Vendor). Previously it was removed from the
    stable list first and then spawned ownerless into the world.

FIXED - Vendor:
  - The server buy price now comes from the selected stock entry's own PRICE tag
    instead of the first same-BaseId entry's price. Two stock entries sharing a
    BaseId at different prices could otherwise let the server charge a different
    price than the client's selected row.
  - The per-item @Buy / @Sell trigger now fires BEFORE the transfer and RETURN 1
    vetoes that line (Source-X). It used to fire after the trade had already
    completed, so its return value was ignored.

FIXED - Secure trade:
  - @TradeAccepted now fires BEFORE any item changes hands; RETURN 1 from either
    party cancels the whole trade and returns the items to their owners (Source-X
    CItemContainer). It used to fire after the swap, so the cancel was a no-op.



FIXED - Ships:
  - Ship components are now classified by their ITEMDEF TYPE (tiller / plank /
    side / hold) instead of always being ShipOther, so steering, boarding planks
    and the cargo hold work on a freshly-placed ship.
  - Diagonal ship commands (SHIPFORELEFT / FORERIGHT / BACKLEFT / BACKRIGHT) move
    the ship diagonally again — the movement direction is no longer collapsed to
    the 4 cardinal directions (only the facing is 4-way).
  - Deck-object selection now gates on Z as well as the XY footprint (Source-X
    CCMultiMovable): an object well above or below the deck (a swimmer under the
    hull, a bird overhead) is no longer dragged along with the ship.

FIXED - Housing:
  - Custom-foundation houses are restored on world load: DeserializeFromWorld now
    reads MultiCustom items, not only Multi. A customized house no longer falls out
    of the house registry after a restart (which left it to decay unmanaged).
  - Persisted lockdown/secure entries are loaded without re-running the live
    capacity checks, so a saved house that holds more than the current
    MaxLockdowns/MaxSecure (config or storage changed since the save) no longer
    silently loses the overflow entries.



FIXED - Regions / Flags:
  - RegionFlag numeric values now match Source-X CRegion.h (NoMagic=0x1, Gate=0x8,
    NoBuild=0x80, Announce=0x200, Underground=0x800, NoDecay=0x1000, Safe=0x2000,
    Guarded=0x4000, NoPvP=0x8000, Arena=0x10000, NoMining=0x20000, plus the
    anti-magic / ship / house / inherit bits). A legacy numeric FLAGS=04000 from a
    Source-X / mortechUO script is now read as Guarded instead of Safe. SphereNet-
    specific flags (Mark/SafeZone/NoPeraCrime/Jail/RedZone/GuardedOff) moved to high
    bits so they never collide with a real REGION_FLAG_* value. All code references
    the flags by name, so behaviour is unchanged for symbolic FLAGS lists.
  - Added the NODECAY region flag: a loose ground item in a NODECAY region no longer
    decays (Source-X REGION_FLAG_NODECAY); it decays normally once it leaves.

FIXED - Spawns:
  - @Spawn that places the NPC at an explicit position is honored — the engine no
    longer re-randomizes the location over a script-chosen spawn point (Source-X
    CCSpawn).
  - Spawned items/NPCs whose placement is refused (out of bounds) are now deleted
    instead of being tracked as orphans with no sector. PlaceItem/PlaceCharacter
    return a success bool for this.
  - A misconfigured char spawner (no chardef and no spawn group) now reschedules
    its timer instead of re-entering and bailing on every item tick of its sector
    (spawn-tick storm).

FIXED - World commands:
  - The RESPAWN and RESTOCK console/IPC/panel commands are now wired to real
    implementations: RESPAWN tops every char/item spawner up to its max
    (independent of sector sleep), RESTOCK fires @NPCRestock on every vendor. They
    previously printed "requested" and did nothing.



FIXED - Notoriety / Murder:
  - The murderer (red) threshold is now strictly greater-than MurderMinCount
    (Source-X Noto_IsMurderer: murders > count), so with the default 5 the red
    title appears on the 6th kill, not the 5th. It was flagging red one kill early.
  - A PvP kill now only counts as a murder when it is an UNPROVOKED kill of an
    innocent (Source-X Noto_Kill: NotoThem < NOTO_GUILD_SAME). Killing a criminal
    or murderer (grey/red), or someone who aggressed the killer first (the killer
    holds a HarmedBy memory of the victim → self-defence), no longer adds a murder
    count or criminal flag. Previously every player-vs-player kill was marked as
    murder + criminal.

FIXED - Notoriety / Fame:
  - The artificial 200-point per-kill fame cap is removed (Source-X Calc_FameKill
    has no per-kill cap, only the 0..10000 running-total clamp, which is still
    applied). Killing a high-fame player now grants the full fame/10.



FIXED - Death / Triggers:
  - @Death and @Kill RETURN 1 are now honored. The firing is centralized in
    DeathEngine.ProcessDeath (every death entry point — combat, spell, NPC, GM,
    reactive-armor — routes through it): @Death RETURN 1 cancels the death entirely
    (no corpse, the victim stays alive), @Kill RETURN 1 skips that killer's credit
    (notoriety/karma/fame/murder/experience) while the death still proceeds.
    Previously the triggers were fired-and-ignored at each call site. An
    invulnerable character also no longer dies (Source-X STATF_INVUL).

FIXED - Death / Forensics:
  - Corpses now stamp DEATH_TIME (and CORPSE_SLEEPING when applicable), and carving
    sets CORPSE_CARVED — the exact tags the Forensics skill reads. Carving used to
    write a "CARVED" tag that was never read back, so Forensics always reported a
    corpse as un-carved with an unknown time of death.

FIXED - Death / Loot retention:
  - Corpse loot transfer now also keeps move-never, no-trade and stays-with-owner
    (cursed2) items on the owner, in addition to blessed/newbie/no-drop. A
    move-never item could previously land in a lootable corpse where no player
    could pick it up.

FIXED - Death / Looting crime:
  - Looting another player's corpse is now wired into the item-pickup path and
    flags the looter criminal (Source-X CheckCorpseCrime). It is correctly gated:
    only a still-present, innocent player owner makes looting a crime — monster
    corpses (the NPC is deleted on death) and criminal/own/party/guild-shared
    corpses are free to loot. The IsLootingCriminal helper was computed but never
    applied at pickup before.



FIXED - Items / Equipment layers:
  - The Layer enum now matches UO LAYER_TYPE numbering: LAYER_FACE=15 and
    LAYER_BEARD(FacialHair)=16 were swapped, which put beards on the face layer
    on the wire and mis-mapped legacy LAYER_BEARD=16 imports onto the Face slot.
    Character-creation beards and legacy beard imports now land on the correct
    layer. LAYER_DRAGGING=31 is defined for numeric parity (dragging is still
    tracked via the DRAGGING tag); the equip-layer validation still rejects the
    internal layers (31+), so client-equippable layers are unchanged.

FIXED - Items / Stack split:
  - Splitting a stack now produces a full clone of the original for the
    left-behind remainder (Source-X CreateDupeItem): custom tags, attribute flags
    (stored as tags), durability/quality, price/link, MORE/MOREB/MOREP, TDATA
    overrides, decay time and the runtime EVENTS list all travel with the split.
    Previously only id/hue/amount/type/name/more1/more2/direction were copied, so
    that state was silently dropped from the remainder.
  - Two piles now only merge when their tag sets match (Source-X CItem::Stack
    compares m_TagDefs and the ATTR_* flags, which SphereNet stores as tags), so
    stacking no longer silently drops one stack's tags.



ADDED - NPC AI / Config:
  - NPCAI, NPCHealThreshold and NPCWanderLookAroundChance are now read from the
    .ini. The global NPC_AI_* flag set is seeded from NPCAI instead of being
    hardcoded; the default stays PATH|COMBAT|PERSISTENTPATH|THREAT (0x0C41) so
    existing worlds keep pathfinding/threat. Set NPCAI=0 for bare Source-X.
  - Per-character OVERRIDE.NPCAI is honored over the global NPCAI mask, so the
    looting/food/path/threat behaviour can be set on a single creature (Source-X
    CCharNPC::GetNpcAiFlags). Looting, IntFood, Path, PersistentPath and Threat
    checks now resolve the per-character flags.

FIXED - NPC AI / Pathfinding:
  - A* pathfinding is gated on intelligence: a creature with effective INT < 30
    no longer routes around obstacles (it faces the target and steps as the line
    opens). NPC_AI_ALWAYSINT bypasses the gate (treated as INT 300). Source-X
    NPC_Pathfinding parity.

FIXED - NPC AI / Special attacks:
  - Breath and rock-throw now require FULL stamina (Source-X
    Stat_GetVal(DEX) >= Stat_GetAdjusted(DEX)) instead of half, so they fire on
    the opening exchange / after a rest rather than every tick.
  - Ogre/ettin/cyclops bodies throw rocks by default when carrying a throwable
    rock (ItemType.ARock/Rock) in their pack; the default throw range is 2-9 (was
    2-8). THROWOBJ/THROWRANGE/THROWDAM tag throwers are unchanged.

FIXED - NPC AI / Spellbooks:
  - NPCs derive their spell list from any spellbook type (necro/paladin/bushido/
    ninjitsu/arcanist/mystic/mastery/extra), reading the book itemdef's spell
    window (TDATA3 offset, TDATA4 max spells) instead of assuming the classic
    64-bit magery book. The classic book remains the fallback when undefined.
    Source-X NPC_AddSpellsFromBook parity.

FIXED - NPC AI / Triggers:
  - @NPCActCast RETURN 1 now aborts the cast and reverts to melee instead of
    being consumed as a successful action (Source-X NPC_FightMagery). The trigger
    receives ARGN1=spell and LOCAL.HealThreshold (from NPCHealThreshold) and may
    override the cast spell via ARGN1.
  - @NPCActFight now receives ARGN1=distance and ARGN2=motivation with ARGO=target
    (was the target UID in ARGN1). A script may flip motivation (ARGN2 readback),
    force a cast via LOCAL.skill + LOCAL.spell, or fully handle the action with
    RETURN 1.
  - Trigger ARGN1/ARGN2/ARGN3 mutations made by a script are now copied back to
    the engine after each character trigger block (was lost before; LOCAL.* was
    already shared), so @NPCActFight/@NPCActCast/@HitTry readbacks work.

[2026-06-30] - Skill/spell parity: flags, caps, gain, Discordance, spells (Wave 151)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Skills / Definitions:
  - SKILLDEF now parses RANGE (gather use-distance) and PROMPT_CLILOC (target
    cursor cliloc); both were silently dropped before.
  - SkillFlag bit values now match Source-X SKF_* (GATHER=0x400, DISABLED=0x800,
    plus IMMOBILE/SELECTABLE/NOMINDIST/NOANIM/NOSFX/RANGED). The previous values
    diverged from 0x10 up and invented NOFAIL/RANKEDTITLE, so a script FLAGS bit
    was misread. SKILLDEF FLAGS now also accepts symbolic, pipe-delimited values
    (e.g. "skf_gather|skf_ranged"), like SPELL/CHARDEF already did.
  - Startup and ReSync logs now report how many spells/itemdefs/chardefs and
    skilldefs were loaded.

FIXED - Skills / Caps and gain:
  - The skill success S-curve variance is now 100 (Source-X SKILL_VARIANCE),
    not 150.
  - Per-character OVERRIDE.SKILLCAP_<n> and OVERRIDE.SKILLSUM tags are honored
    over the skill-class and global caps.
  - Skill gain no longer advances inside Safe regions (Source-X parity).

FIXED - Magic / Skills:
  - Casting awards the caster's casting-skill a gain attempt on every resolved
    cast, success or fizzle (previously the casting skill never advanced).
  - @SkillUseQuick now fires AFTER the success roll with ARGN3 = result; a script
    can flip the result or cancel the use (RETURN 1). It used to fire before the
    roll and could only hard-cancel.

ADDED - Skills:
  - Discordance/Enticement is now a working skill: it requires a musical
    instrument and a Musicianship+Discordance check, then temporarily lowers the
    target's defenses.
  - Crafting tools take durability damage on each craft attempt.

ADDED / FIXED - Magic:
  - Magic Lock / Unlock now lock and unlock containers and doors; Magic Trap /
    Untrap set and clear the trapped state; Arch Protection and Mass Curse now
    apply their group buff/curse (they were inert).
  - Reactive Armor now reflects a quarter of spell damage back at the caster, as
    it already did for melee.
  - A harmful spell cast on an innocent player now flags the caster criminal,
    matching a melee attack.
  - Teleport now validates the destination (off-map / impassable tile) like
    Recall and Gate, so it can no longer strand the caster in a wall.

[2026-06-30] - Combat parity: flags, scriptable damage/parry, ammo and skill overrides (Wave 150)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Combat / Flags:
  - Several COMBATFLAGS that were defined but inert now affect the swing path:
    NODIRCHANGE (the attacker no longer auto-rotates to face the target),
    ARCHERYCANMOVE (archers may fire without waiting out the post-move settle
    delay), PARALYZE_CANSWING (a paralyzed/frozen attacker can keep swinging;
    sleep still blocks), and STACKARMOR (a body region covered by several worn
    pieces sums all their AR instead of only the primary layer's).
  - NPC_BONUSDAMAGE: a Damage Increase % (INCREASEDAM tag, Source-X
    PROPCH_INCREASEDAM, capped at ±100%) applies to players always and to NPCs
    only when this flag is set.

ADDED - Combat / Scripting:
  - @Hit, @GetHit and the weapon/armor item hooks now fire after armor/parry but
    BEFORE damage is applied to HP, so a script can raise, lower or cancel the
    damage via ARGN1 (RETURN 1 cancels). These fire from one shared pipeline used
    by both the player and NPC swing paths; previously they fired after HP was
    already applied, where a script could observe but not modify the damage.
  - The NPC swing path now fires @HitTry (adjust swing delay / abort) and
    @HitCheck (force a miss) before resolving, matching the player path.
  - Parry is now scriptable: a successful parry fires @HitParry and may let part
    of the damage leak through (ARGN1), instead of always being a full block.
  - Weapon skill override: a weapon may declare a non-default combat skill via
    TAG.OVERRIDE_SKILL (e.g. wield a blade with Fencing).

ADDED - Combat / Ranged:
  - Ranged weapons honor their ITEMDEF AMMOTYPE (which exact ammo item is
    consumed) and AMMOANIM (the in-flight projectile graphic). When a weapon def
    specifies neither, the legacy arrow-for-bows / bolt-for-crossbows defaults
    still apply.

[2026-06-29] - World object unlink, region cache and ground stack merge fixes (Wave 149)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - World / Object lifecycle:
  - High-level delete paths (script REMOVE, equipped-layer FINDLAYER().REMOVE,
    container DELETE/EMPTY, and consumable item use such as food, deeds, drinks
    and seeds) called the low-level Item.Delete() flag-set, which only marked the
    item deleted and cleared its own contents. The item stayed registered in the
    world object table (its serial was never freed) and, for worn items, lingered
    in the wearer's equipment slot — dead references that inflated object counts
    and could surface as a deleted item still counting toward equipment/weight.
    These paths now route through the full world removal, which unlinks the item
    from the object table, parent container, equipment slot and sector. Object
    teardown also clears the wearer's layer when an equipped item is removed.

FIXED - World / Regions:
  - FindRegion cached lookups per 8x8 tile cell but also stored null (no-region)
    results. Region edges are not 8-aligned, so a single cell can straddle a
    boundary; a region-less query then poisoned the cell and a later in-region
    query for another tile in the same cell wrongly returned null. This could let
    region-gated behavior (guarded, no-PvP, no-magic, enter/leave, gathering,
    weather) lapse near boundaries. Only successful lookups are cached now;
    non-region tiles re-resolve, and cached hits stay self-validating.

FIXED - Items / Inventory:
  - Merging a dragged stack onto a target stack that sits on the ground sent a
    container-content packet addressed to the ground item itself, desyncing its
    amount label. The merged ground pile now broadcasts a world item update, and
    any overflow remainder drops to the ground beside it instead of being lost.

FIXED - Host / Stability:
  - The Host had no last-resort handler for unhandled exceptions on background
    threads. The child server's output is mirrored to the console on an
    AsyncStreamReader thread with no surrounding try/catch, so when the console
    handle became invalid mid-run (an interactive/RDP session disconnecting, or
    redirected stdout) the resulting IOException went unhandled and terminated
    the Host, taking the child game server down with it and leaving only a
    0xe0434352 in the event log. Console mirroring now swallows IOException and
    InvalidOperationException, and a global handler persists any unhandled
    exception to logs/host-crash.log.

FIXED - Memory:
  - Server and Host now build with Workstation GC instead of Server GC. On the
    low-core/low-RAM VDS deployment target Server GC keeps a per-CPU heap and
    holds committed segments, so RSS climbed steadily under a steady allocation
    rate and read as a leak even with a single player.
  - NetState releases its grown per-connection send and crypt scratch buffers
    back to their initial sizes when a connection is cleared, so a transient
    large broadcast no longer pins that memory for the life of the slot.

SECURITY:
  - Pinned the native SQLite binary (SQLitePCLRaw.lib.e_sqlite3 3.50.3) above
    the 2.1.11 pulled in transitively by Microsoft.Data.Sqlite, clearing
    advisory GHSA-2m69-gcr7-jv3q (NU1903). The package is native-only, so the
    managed SQLitePCLRaw core/provider ABI is unchanged.

[2026-06-15] - Stack splitting and item weight system fixes (Wave 148)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Items / Inventory:
  - Partial stack pickup marked the newly-created serial as the dragged item,
    while the client continues dropping with the clicked source serial, matching
    Source-X / ServUO behavior. That mismatch made the split-off item disappear
    and produced 0x28/05 "item does not exist" responses. The clicked serial now
    remains held with the picked amount, and a new leftover stack is created at
    the old container/ground location.
  - Stack-on-stack merge no longer relies on setting an item amount to zero,
    which was clamped back to one and could leave a phantom item. Fully moved
    stacks are removed from the world; overflow remains as a positive amount.
  - Ground pile items such as arrows, gold and bandages no longer get FLIP/DIR
    visual changes on drop. They keep the base graphic, and SA clients receive
    the 0xF3 world item packet with correct direction and amount fields.

FIXED - Items / Weight:
  - ITEMDEF WEIGHT parsing now matches Source-X: integer values are whole stones
    converted to internal tenths (WEIGHT=2 => 20), and decimal values parse
    correctly (WEIGHT=0.5 => 5). Previously a 1-stone item could display/count
    as 0 stones, and decimal weights were ineffective.
  - Container, bank, trade, status/tooltip and stealing weight calculations now
    use consistent units. Capacity checks compare tenths to tenths, while
    player-facing weight values are reported in whole stones.
  - Items explicitly defined with WEIGHT=0 stay weightless, while undefined
    items use tiledata or a minimal fallback instead of becoming weightless.

[2026-06-14] - Vendor stock no longer doubles on restock (Wave 147)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Vendor:
  - Repopulating a vendor's virtual stock (SELL= / PopulateVendorStock) appended
    to the existing pack without clearing it, so the periodic @NPCRestock (every
    10 minutes) and any re-run of SELL= over an already-stocked vendor stacked a
    second copy of every row — the same item showing up twice in the buy gump,
    compounding on each restock and inflating the in-memory item count. A restock
    now clears the existing virtual stock before refilling to the template
    levels, matching Source-X NPC_Vendor_Restock.

[2026-06-14] - Two-handed weapons equip on the TwoHanded layer (Wave 146)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Combat / Equipment:
  - A two-handed weapon (TWOHANDS=Y: bows, crossbows, two-handed swords/axes/
    maces, halberds, …) was equipping on the OneHanded layer because UO tiledata
    marks some of them there. The client picks the attack animation from the
    equipped layer, so a bow on OneHanded swung like an empty-handed punch and a
    two-handed melee weapon used a one-handed swing. Character.Equip now promotes
    such weapons to the TwoHanded layer (Source-X LAYER_HAND2) and the worn-item
    packet reports the actual layer.
  - The swing animation's one/two-handed choice now keys on IsTwoHanded
    (itemdef TWOHANDS) rather than the layer alone, so a two-hander animates
    correctly even if a save predates the layer promotion. The unmatched weapon
    case now falls back to BASH, matching Source-X GenerateAnimate.

[2026-06-14] - Honor the picked starting city on character creation (Wave 145)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Character creation:
  - The starting city the player picked was ignored — new characters always
    spawned at city index 0 (Yew), so choosing Britain still dropped you in Yew.
    The create-character packet (0x00/0xF8) now reads the city index, and the
    character spawns at the matching city from the 0xA9 list the client was shown.

[2026-06-14] - Pile item display: amount label + ore-only graphic ramp (Wave 144)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Items / Display:
  - Stacked pile items now show their amount on the single-click label and the
    property tooltip ("1234 gold coins"), via Item.GetDisplayName, matching
    Source-X CItem::GetNameFull. Single items (and non-piles) show just the name.

FIXED - Items / Graphics:
  - Only ore now changes graphic with stack size (ITEMID_ORE_1..4 per Source-X
    CItem::SetAmount); arrows, bandages, ingots, gold and other piles keep their
    base graphic and let the client render the count. The previous DUPELIST-based
    amount ramp wrongly reskinned stacked arrows/bandages, whose DUPELIST is a
    flip/alias list, not a size ramp. Also fixes an ItemType<->DispIdFull
    recursion the ore check would otherwise trigger.

[2026-06-14] - Armed-creature double hit sound fix (Wave 143)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Combat / Sound:
  - An armed creature played both its own CharDef attack sound and the weapon
    hit sound on a hit (doubling up). Per Source-X SoundChar(CRESND_HIT) an armed
    strike makes only the weapon sound, so the creature attack vocalization now
    falls back only when the attacker is unarmed; an armed creature plays just the
    weapon sound.

[2026-06-14] - Defender pain sound, absorbed-hit feedback, parry spark (Wave 142)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Combat / Sound:
  - A struck target now plays its pain vocalization (Source-X CRESND_GETHIT):
    creatures use their CharDef SOUNDGETHIT, humans use the gendered "oomf" set
    (male 0x154-0x159, female 0x14B-0x14F). Emitted on a damaging hit from both
    the player and NPC paths; players previously had no get-hit sound at all.
    The NPC creature get-hit emission was unified into the hit feedback so it now
    covers creature and player targets alike without doubling.

FIXED - Combat / Hit resolution:
  - A connecting hit that armor fully absorbed (0 damage) was reported as a miss,
    so it played the miss whoosh with no get-hit animation. ResolveAttack now
    returns -1 for a true miss/parry and 0 for an absorbed hit, so the player and
    NPC paths play the weapon hit sound and get-hit animation for an absorbed hit
    (no pain sound, damage number or blood), matching Source-X Fight_Hit.

ADDED - Combat / Visuals:
  - A successful parry/block now shows a spark on the defender (ModernUO 0x37B9);
    previously a parry produced no client feedback at all.

FIXED - Combat / Sound:
  - The NPC weapon hit sound is now only played when the attacker is armed, so an
    unarmed creature no longer overlays a human fist sound on top of its own
    CharDef attack sound.

[2026-06-14] - Per-weapon hit/miss combat sounds (Wave 141)
----------------------------------------

CHANGED - Combat / Sound:
  - Melee and ranged swings now play a per-weapon hit or miss sound instead of a
    single generic thud/clang. Hit sounds follow Source-X SoundChar(CRESND_HIT)
    by weapon class (mace 0x233, war axe 0x232, two-handed sword/axe 0x236/0x237,
    one-handed sword/axe and fencing 0x23B/0x23C, bow/crossbow 0x234, throwing
    0x5D2, whip 0x67E, unarmed 0x135). Miss sounds draw at random from the
    Source-X ranged set {0x233,0x238} or melee set {0x238,0x239,0x23A}.
  - A swing now emits exactly one combat sound (hit OR miss), matching Source-X
    Fight_Hit. The previous unconditional swing whoosh that played on top of the
    hit/miss sound (doubling up) was removed from the player and NPC paths, and
    the forced-miss feedback no longer plays two stacked sounds.

[2026-06-14] - Moving-bolt effect direction (oneDirection) fix (Wave 140)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Combat / Visuals:
  - The graphical-effect packet (0x70) always wrote the oneDirection byte as
    true, so moving EFFECT_BOLT projectiles (arrows, bolts, energy bolt, magic
    arrow, throwing) did not rotate to face their flight path and looked wrong.
    Source-X writeBasicEffect (and ModernUO MovingParticles) only set
    oneDirection for stationary effects; bolts use false. The direction byte is
    now derived from the effect type (false for type 0 / EFFECT_BOLT, true
    otherwise) across the player ranged shot, the NPC ranged shot, and the
    script/character EFFECT emitters.

FIXED - Combat / Blood:
  - The blood-splatter graphic set was missing 0x1645 (BLOOD_SPLAT); it is now
    included to match the Source-X / ModernUO blood pool.

[2026-06-14] - Combat blood splatter + NPC ranged projectile (Wave 139)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Combat / Visuals:
  - Landing a hit now scatters 1-2 short-lived blood items around the struck
    target (graphics 0x122A-0x122F), hued by the target's CharDef BLOODCOLOR and
    decaying after 5 seconds. Emitted on both the player and NPC hit paths via a
    shared GameClient.EmitBloodSplat helper; placed as ground items so the
    view-delta renders them.
  - NPC archers now emit the moving arrow/bolt projectile when they fire a bow
    or crossbow (bow -> 0x0F3F arrow, crossbow -> 0x1BFB bolt), mirroring the
    player's ranged effect. Previously only players showed the flying ammo.

[2026-06-14] - Stack-merge gold loss, mining depletion, pile graphics, archery loop + swing anims (Wave 138)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Inventory / Stacking:
  - Dropping one stack onto a matching stack treated the target stack as a
    container and nested the dragged item inside it (invisible), so stacking
    gold onto gold lost the dropped pile. It now merges the amounts; an overflow
    tops the target off and keeps the remainder beside it.

FIXED - Skills / Mining:
  - The resource-depletion marker tracked its remaining pool in Item.Amount,
    which floors at 1, so a node never reached 0 and yielded ore forever. The
    pool is now stored in a tag, so veins deplete and then regenerate on the
    regen timer.

FIXED - Items / Display:
  - Stackable "pile" items (ore, ingot, log, bandage, scroll, arrow, ...) show a
    larger graphic as the amount grows, driven by DUPELIST (Source-X parity).
    Gated on pile-ness so DUPELIST used for animation/variant frames on non-pile
    items is unaffected. Computed in DispIdFull, so every packet path and the
    view-delta refresh the visual when the amount changes.

FIXED - Combat:
  - Firing a ranged weapon with no ammo returned without advancing the swing
    timer, so the combat tick re-entered every server tick — spamming the
    no-ammo message and looping. It now paces by the swing timer like Source-X.
  - Swing animation by weapon type: axe and pickaxe SLASH (were on the
    pierce/bash paths) and throwing weapons use the 1H-slash gesture, matching
    Source-X CChar::GenerateAnimate.

CHANGED - Admin:
  - Serv.AllClients runs a function-form payload (e.g. f_Admin_GetPlayers) as a
    script function first, before trying it as a verb, with the issuer as SRC.
    Added an [allclients] diagnostic for the online-player tally.

[2026-06-14] - Console memory cap, vendor double-stock, item name fallback, spell power words (Wave 137)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Console / Memory:
  - The GUI console's pending-line queue had no cap. With packet debug logging
    on, lines were enqueued faster than the UI thread could render them, so the
    backlog grew without bound and process RAM climbed into the gigabytes over
    hours. The queue is now capped; lines past the cap are dropped and the count
    is surfaced in the console.

FIXED - Vendors:
  - Opening a vendor whose stock was empty ran BOTH the persisted-tag rebuild
    and the @NPCRestock script trigger, spawning the SELL list twice — every buy
    row appeared doubled. The trigger now only fires when the rebuild produced
    nothing.

FIXED - Items:
  - Item.GetName falls back to the tiledata tile name (resolved and pluralized)
    when neither a per-instance name nor an itemdef NAME= is set. An item such
    as i_bottle_empty (no NAME=) had been reaching the client with an empty
    name, so the client rendered its own raw tiledata string with the plural
    marker intact ("empty bottle %s%").

FIXED - Magic:
  - Spell power words spoke the legacy letter abbreviation ("IL") for spells
    whose RUNES only carry it. GetPowerWords now uses the spoken word form when
    present and otherwise falls back to the canonical UO mantra ("In Lor"), so
    the player and NPC cast paths read the same words.

[2026-06-14] - NPC casting, creature attacks, packet ordering, view-sync, character creation (Wave 136)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Magic / NPC AI:
  - NPC casters were exempted from the reagent-availability gate; an NPC with
    an empty pack could never start a cast (every attempt returned failure).
  - NPCSPELL now parses a spell defname/enum name, not only a numeric id;
    numeric spell-type values are range-checked and cast to the enum's ushort
    base before Enum.IsDefined (a numeric NPCSPELL/SPELL value crashed the world
    loader with an ArgumentException).
  - Spell selection no longer re-casts Paralyze on an already-frozen target and
    enforces a per-caster Paralyze cooldown, so a caster stops looping on
    Paralyze (including against a target that breaks free instantly) and unloads
    damage between locks.
  - Self-heal chance is a flat 33% at any wound level, so a critically hurt
    caster spends ~2/3 of its casts on offense instead of turtling.
  - Mana regen uses a flat base amount instead of INT/50; a high-INT caster no
    longer regenerated mana as fast as it spent it and now actually runs dry.

FIXED - Combat / Creatures:
  - Venomous NPCs (Poisoning skill > 0) envenom on a melee hit from the skill
    alone, with no poisoned-weapon tag required.
  - Special movement trail: giant spiders web the ground and fire elementals
    drop fire patches (FIELD_DAMAGE) as they act; driven by body id or the
    WEBTRAIL/FIRETRAIL tag. Fire-elemental body id corrected to 0x000F.

FIXED - Network / packet ordering:
  - The 0x2E worn-item packet no longer sets the 0x8000 hue-flag bit on the
    graphic (that convention belongs to the 0x78 equipment list); a worn item
    with a non-zero hue was sent with an invalid graphic and vanished on the
    client until a resync.
  - Vendor buy/sell lists (0x74/0x9E) and spellbook content (0xD4) are Normal
    priority again. The send queue drains Highest->Low, so a Low member of an
    order-critical sequence flushed after the Normal open-container packet that
    consumes it: vendor rows showed 0gp with no name and spellbooks opened
    empty.

FIXED - View-delta / appearance sync:
  - Dyeing a worn item, and hair/beard dye, now broadcast the recolour; the
    ground-item view-delta never tracks worn items, so the change stayed the old
    colour for everyone until a resync.
  - Criminal/murderer state is part of the view-delta visibility key, so a
    stationary attacker turns grey/red on observers without having to move.

FIXED - Character creation:
  - [STARTSGOLD] bare-amount rows are parsed (the amount is the section key);
    new characters receive one stipend (the start-index row) instead of nothing.
  - Item single-click labels and tooltips fall back to the itemdef NAME= when no
    per-instance name was stamped, so plain spawned/looted items show their name.

[2026-06-13] - Ping fast-path processing (Wave 135)
----------------------------------------

IMPROVED - Network / RTT:
  - 0x73 ping packets now bypass the generic packet-buffer copy path and go
    directly through echo/RTT handling.
  - Added regression coverage for the ping fast path through the real
    NetworkManager parser.

























[2026-06-13] - ClassicUO death scene and corpse binding (Wave 134)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Death / ClassicUO:
  - Player corpse OWNER/KILLER tags are now written before the
    DeathEngine OnDeath callback, so the GameClient death sequence can
    find the corpse by OWNER_UID and bind to the correct serial.
  - The dying player's own client now receives a 0xAF DeathAnimation
    packet with a non-zero corpse serial. This completes the
    death-screen flow that ClassicUO needs to transition mobile ->
    corpse instead of leaving the live sprite stuck or failing to open
    the "you are dead" scene.
  - Added regression coverage for the DeathEngine owner-tag order and
    the self death-animation packet.

[2026-06-11] - @SpellEffectTick bridge; ship @RegionEnter/@RegionLeave; shared trigger LOCAL pool (Wave 133)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Scripting engine:
  - Shared trigger LOCAL pool (Source-X CScriptTriggerArgs.m_VarsLocal
    parity): TriggerArgs can now carry one VarMap that every ON=@X
    block in a trigger chain uses as its scope locals — the engine
    seeds values before the fire and reads script writes back after.
    Functions keep their own locals (Source-X call semantics).
  - @SpellEffectTick (SPELLFLAG_TICK) fires from the native poison
    tick: ARGN1 = spell id, ARGN2 = strength on the Sphere memory
    scale, ARGO = a read-only spell-memory shim (BASEID = the spell's
    RUNE_ITEM, MOREY = strength, LINK = poisoner) so the reference
    handler pattern IF (<ARGO.BASEID>==I_RUNE_POISON) works verbatim.
    LOCAL.EFFECT/DELAY/CHARGES/DAMAGETYPE are seeded and read back;
    the script damage applies as-is (no second resist pass), zero
    damage skips the application but keeps the schedule, RETURN 1
    destroys the effect (cures). IsTrigUsed-gated: unhooked shards
    pay a null check per tick.
  - Item @RegionLeave/@RegionEnter wired with Source-X scope — these
    fire on movable multis, not ordinary items: ShipEngine.MoveDelta
    checks the multi anchor's region BEFORE anything moves; on a
    boundary cross the triggers fire on the ship multi with ARGO =
    region and SRC = pilot, and RETURN 1 blocks the whole step.
    Installed only when hooked.

FIXED - Networking (minor):
  - NetState.SendRaw built its buffer one WriteByte per byte; now a
    single block copy (cold path — script SENDPACKET verb).

[2026-06-11] - NPC attack-engagement emote (Wave 132)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - NPC AI / Combat:
  - The "*X is attacking Y!*" / "*X is attacking you!*" emote pair
    (reference Attacker_Add messaging) only existed on the player
    attack path — an NPC engaging a player produced no announcement
    at all, so an aggressor closing in gave no visual warning. NpcAI
    now raises OnNpcAttackNotify the first combat action against a
    new target (past the flee/leash give-up branches, before the
    first swing), and the server broadcasts the same emote pair as
    the player path: observers get the third-person line, the victim
    alone gets the "attacking you" variant, both over the attacker
    in the emote hue. The notify latch re-fires only on target
    switch and is swept with the other per-NPC AI state.

[2026-06-11] - NPC pathfind fail-backoff; main-loop stall diagnostics (Wave 131)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - NPC AI / Performance:
  - A failed combat-chase A* (unreachable target) burns the entire
    node budget before giving up, and the recompute throttle allowed
    a retry every 750ms — each NPC stuck behind an unwalkable area
    stalled the single-threaded apply phase 40-75ms per attempt
    (2000 nodes at ~35us/node), visible as ~160ms ping spikes.
    Failed computes now back off for 5s (successful ones keep the
    750ms cadence) and the node budget drops to 500, bounding the
    worst case to ~17ms. The direct-step fast path above A* still
    runs every action, so the NPC resumes immediately once the
    straight line opens.

ADDED - Diagnostics:
  - [loop_stall] warning: any main-loop iteration over 50ms logs a
    per-segment breakdown (console/actions, network input, periodic
    jobs, network output, server ticks, yield) plus GC gen0/1/2
    collection deltas, rate-limited to one log per 2s. Catches
    latency the tick telemetry cannot see — ticks cover <1% of
    iteration wall time, so tick_stats can read 0.2ms avg while the
    ping echo spikes.

[2026-06-11] - Panel dialog designer with live MUL-art preview (Wave 130)
----------------------------------------

ADDED - Admin panel / Tooling:
  - GumpArtReader decodes gumpidx.mul + gumpart.mul (per-row RLE,
    16-bit 555) to RGBA; a dependency-free PNG encoder serves the art
    over HTTP with caching.
  - Panel endpoints: /gumpart/{id}.png (gump art, outside /api so
    <img> tags work), /api/dialogs (all loaded [DIALOG] names),
    /api/dialog-source?name= (raw section text read from the script

  - GumpDesignerPage rebuilt: real gump art on the canvas (RESIZEPIC
    as a true 9-slice, GUMPPIC/BUTTON/CHECKBOX/RADIO images, tiled

    live. Existing dialogs load from the server and import onto the

  - The status port also serves /dialogedit — a standalone

    build.

[2026-06-11] - Resource markers use the worldgem-bit graphic (Wave 129)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Gathering:
  - Per-tile resource markers (region pool and fallback) were created
    with the 0x1 "nodraw" graphic, which renders nothing even for
    staff with AllShow — veins could not be seen or inspected. Both
    marker systems now use the reference worldgem-bit graphic (0x1EA7)
    named "worldgem bit"; ATTR_INVIS still hides them from players.
    Consumption itself was already pool-limited per tile with a regen

[2026-06-11] - Character creation: outfit, per-skill kits, setup functions (Wave 128)
----------------------------------------

FIXED - Character creation:
  - NEWBIE race variants ("[NEWBIE MALE_DEFAULT ELF]"/GARG — usually
    empty) were keyed by their first token and overwrote the human
    base section, so MALE/FEMALE_DEFAULT resolved to an empty section
    and fresh characters spawned naked. The race suffix now folds into
    the section identity; the default outfit equips again.
  - Each chosen creation skill now grants its [NEWBIE <SKILL>] starter
    kit on top of the default outfit (unknown names no-op).
  - New player characters run the pack setup chain
    f_onchar_create_player → f_onchar_setup_player (Char_Start_Player:
